Current Commentary

Opening of the Fifth Plenary Session

The Fifth Plenary Session of the Central Committee opened yesterday in the capital. It has been exactly one year since the previous Fourth Plenary Session was convened. During this year, although the international situation has become increasingly tense, the domestic political situation has gradually become more stable. The Fujian Incident had already concluded around the time of the Fourth Plenary Session, and the conflict between Ningbian's Sun and Ma was also quelled. Leaders from all sides have generally been able to recognize their own positions and have cooperated sincerely to safeguard this troubled nation. Other achievements, such as the progress in abolishing excessive taxes, the revision of educational policies, and the advancement of transportation construction, can all be commended by the people of the country and cited as facts that, during this period of national crisis, can provide some comfort and reassurance. Recently, the Red bandits entrenched in the southeast have suffered a severe crackdown and fled westward in disarray, becoming spent arrows. What should be focused on in the future is only the issue of how to manage the aftermath in the bandit areas. If there are no ravages of floods, droughts, or natural disasters, then this year can be said to be one of the most stable years since the outbreak of the national crisis, and it can also be said to be the year in which efforts to reorganize domestic affairs began. The Fifth Plenary Session is being convened at the end of this year, allowing the participants to concentrate and calmly discuss major plans for national salvation and survival. What is especially gratifying is that the leaders in the southwest, after Wang and Sun went to Hong Kong to negotiate, have reportedly recognized the necessity of unity and expressed their understanding. Therefore, the convening of this Fifth Plenary Session is truly a key to the whole country rising up in unison to save the nation and lay the foundation for an unshakeable state.

We have always firmly believed that China will not collapse from this setback. We also do not believe that all of our people, from top to bottom, lack the sincerity and determination to strive for progress and revitalize the country. Therefore, we have high hopes for this conference. Moreover, it is reported that the number of attendees at this session has exceeded that of previous sessions, and that the proposals from the various committees do not focus on empty rhetoric but emphasize the telegrams from Wang and Chiang. This especially demonstrates that everyone is determined to be pragmatic and does not want to use vague and hollow discussions as mere embellishments for the meeting. The telegrams first stated, "Today, the way to save the country lies in unity, and the key to achieving unity lies in peace." This is a consistent position of the people of the country, and there can be no disagreement. As for the system of balanced power as the supreme principle for dividing the powers between the central and local governments, it is clearly stipulated in Sun Yat-sen's Outline of National Reconstruction. In the future, if we want to seek a compromise between the two trends of decentralization and centralization, this is the only way to go. The concrete measures for implementing the system of balanced power are already included in the five recommendations outlined in the telegrams, which are concise and essential. From the perspective of those responsible for the central military and political affairs, this clear and distinct joint declaration is of profound significance, far beyond what words can encompass. If the various committees, when discussing the telegrams, can follow these recommendations and plan in advance the methods and steps for implementation, and use the spirit and means of peaceful unification to eliminate various real obstacles, then the achievements of this meeting will surely surpass those of previous meetings. As for the constitution, it is the fundamental law of the country and must be completed as soon as possible so that it can be implemented after being passed by the National Assembly in the future. In this way, the aspiration to end the period of tutelage and implement constitutional government, which has been prepared for several years, can also be achieved. Chairman Chiang said, "If we can apply the same united mindset that we had toward suppressing the communists to saving the country, I dare to believe that any nation in crisis can be saved by the unified mindset of our people." These words suggest that all members of the Central Committee deeply share this sentiment, and the opportunity for peaceful unification lies in this. This is also what we eagerly await.

Japanese Involved in Singapore Espionage Case to Be Deported

Several Japanese Nationals Currently Detained

Japanese Residences Still Being Searched

Naval Exercises Strictly Confidential

Singapore – Singapore is filled with restrained excitement today due to the recent reports of Japanese espionage. All official news has been banned from publication through a semi-official censorship. Governor Thomas has requested that the press immediately cease reporting on this matter, and local officials are also remaining silent. However, the search of Japanese residences continues today, and several Japanese nationals have been detained by the police and are being prepared for deportation. Although officials are maintaining strict secrecy, the general public believes that the police have uncovered spies seeking secret information about Singapore's defenses, most importantly the plans for naval and air force bases in the northeast and army development. (National Telegram, 9th)

Singapore – British naval exercises are scheduled to take place here on Thursday. The content is being kept strictly confidential. Plans and news related to the exercises will be announced to local residents during the exercises. Currently, due to the rampant espionage case, nothing is known. British battleships, destroyers, cruisers, and aircraft will participate in the naval and air exercises to test the defenses of the recently expanded Singapore fortress. These exercises aim to test whether the naval and land forces can withstand an enemy attack. The residents of Singapore are in a state of great anxiety due to the impending exercises and the unresolved espionage case. The police and other authorities are also being tight-lipped about the investigation into Japanese spies. (National Telegram, 10th)

U.S. Navy Report States Warships Must Still Be Stationed in China

(Washington) – Rear Admiral Stanley, Director of the Navy Department's Personnel Bureau, today released his annual report for the period ending June 30, 1934. It placed considerable emphasis on the conditions and achievements of the U.S. Asiatic Fleet over the past year. Admiral Stanley stated that it is still necessary for U.S. warships to be stationed in China. Regarding general naval issues, he advocated that the various fleets should remain stationed in their current locations. He also stated that increasing naval personnel is extremely important, as new ships are currently being built and require skilled personnel to manage them. Stanley's report was submitted directly to Secretary of the Navy Swanson, who will then forward it to President Roosevelt and the Senate Naval Affairs Committee. (National Telegram, 9th)

Yuehan Railway Purchases Materials from England

(London) – The Purchasing Committee of the Central Government has purchased railway equipment in England for the Yuehan Railway. A certain company has contracted to provide various equipment worth £5,000, as well as three bridges worth £41,500. There are also other items. The committee will need to continue purchasing in England soon. (Reuters Telegram, 10th)

France Decides to Refuse Payment of U.S. Debt

(Paris) – The Council of State met this morning to discuss issues related to war debts to the United States. It was decided to maintain the position adopted by the Finance Ministry of refusing to pay. Minister Heillieu declared that he remains committed to his previous position on resolving the war debt issue. (Havas Telegram, 10th)

British Representative's Mediation Succeeds, Central European Situation Relaxes

Yugoslavia Stops Expelling Hungarian Residents

League of Nations Asks Hungary to Reinvestigate

(Geneva) – The Yugoslav-Hungarian issue is quite optimistic today. Relations between the two countries have been extremely strained recently. It is now learned that a conciliation plan is underway, which will advise Hungary to reinvestigate certain officials who encouraged the Yugoslav terrorist party. If the crimes are confirmed, they should be punished. Although France is advocating for Yugoslavia and Italy is supporting Hungary, the representatives of France and Italy in Geneva now have a good understanding. This is the most promising aspect of the situation. As for British neutrality, it is of course unquestionable. It is expected that British representative Eden will be appointed as a public arbitrator. This afternoon, French Foreign Minister Laval submitted a proposal to the League of Nations for consideration. The document is sixty pages long and advocates for the establishment of the right of pursuit and the handling of political prisoners, and proposes the establishment of an international court to deal with political crimes that affect international relations. (Reuters Telegram, 10th)

Belgrade – Yugoslav Minister of the Interior Lazic today ordered that the expulsion of Hungarian residents must be stopped immediately. Those whose residence permits in Yugoslavia have expired are also not to be expelled. It is said that the expulsion of Hungarian residents was largely due to local officials being overly zealous in implementing regulations on foreigners.

According to a Reuters correspondent in Geneva, the Yugoslav government's halt to the expulsion of Hungarian residents has eased the tense situation. The British Lord Privy Seal Eden's admonitions at the League of Nations Administrative Council yesterday must have played a powerful role in the South government's actions. (Reuters Telegram, 9th)

British, French, and Italian Representatives Draft Mediation Measures

Views of Both Sides Gradually Converging

(Geneva) – British representative Eden met here today with Italian representative Aloisi and Hungarian Foreign Minister Kanya for a long time. In the evening, Eden also dined with French Foreign Minister Laval and Czech Foreign Minister Benes. Legal experts from Britain and France were also meeting. Representatives from Yugoslavia and its allies also visited French Foreign Minister Laval this afternoon to discuss the urgent situation. The delegations from Britain, France, and Italy are currently drafting a resolution that could be the first step toward an understanding in the Yugoslav-Hungarian dispute. Eden will continue talks with all parties tomorrow. The situation seems to be improving slightly. It has been generally decided that Eden will be the League of Nations rapporteur for the Yugoslav-Hungarian issue.

The current situation has divided the countries into two factions. France wants the League of Nations to make a decision immediately, believing that the longer the dispute drags on, the greater the danger, as an unfortunate incident may draw Italy into the vortex. Britain advocates a wait-and-see approach and opposes the League of Nations making a hasty decision. However, none of the representatives from Yugoslavia, Czechia, or Romania are willing to accept the British representative's advice. It is expected that Romanian Foreign Minister Titulescu will deliver a passionate speech at the League of Nations Administrative Council meeting tomorrow. The Administrative Council adjourned its meeting yesterday until 3:15 p.m. tomorrow to allow the representatives to talk to each other and ease the somewhat heated atmosphere.

It is reported that the Yugoslav government is requesting that the resolution mention the responsibility of certain Hungarian officials, but does not want to make it difficult for the Hungarian government or the entire country of Hungary. It has also implicitly indicated that if the South government cannot fulfill this wish, it will withdraw its petition to the League of Nations and sever all relations with Hungary in order to achieve satisfaction.

At the same time, the representatives of the Little Entente and the Balkan Entente expressed dissatisfaction with the speeches at yesterday's meeting of the League of Nations Administrative Council. They all felt that the League of Nations Administrative Council completely ignored the evidence presented in the Yugoslav government's memorandum and only made empty talk of condemnation regarding the Marseille assassination, which cannot quell public anger. (Reuters Telegram, 9th)

British and French Agree on Three Key Points of Draft Resolution

Likely to Be Accepted by All Parties

(Geneva) – Since the Yugoslav-Hungarian dispute was submitted to the League of Nations Administrative Council, it has been quite difficult to resolve. Recently, many people have been pessimistic. However, since French Foreign Minister Laval and British Lord Privy Seal Eden met yesterday, the situation has clearly become more relaxed. It is generally believed that Eden has accepted the three key points of the draft resolution proposed by France, which should satisfy the demands of Yugoslavia, namely: (1) Using general language to condemn terrorism, (2) Invoking Article 10 of the League of Nations Covenant, stating that member states have an obligation to respect and maintain the territorial integrity and political independence of all member states, and (3) Hungary should restart the investigation into the responsibility for the Marseille assassination. It is reported that the representatives of Britain, France, and the Little Entente countries agreed on the above points last night. Only Italy and Hungary need to agree. Therefore, Eden met with the representatives of Italy and Hungary this morning and went to Laval's residence at noon. Laval also immediately convened the representatives of the Little Entente countries for joint discussions. (Havas Telegram, 10th)

(Geneva) – It is reported that the League of Nations Administrative Council will appoint a small committee to consider the proposal submitted by French Foreign Minister Laval. According to the current situation, the highest power to pardon anyone accused will be in the hands of the League of Nations. (Reuters Telegram, 10th)

French Foreign Minister Advocates for the Establishment of an International Convention

To Suppress Terrorism

(Geneva) – Today, French Foreign Minister Laval met with the representatives of Greece, Yugoslavia, Italy, Britain, and Czechia one after another, but has not yet reached a solution that can be accepted by both Hungary and Yugoslavia. Laval is enthusiastically supporting Yugoslavia and strongly advocating for the establishment of international measures to suppress acts of terrorism, so that cases like the one in Marseille will not happen again. The British and Italian representatives agreed with Laval that a solution acceptable to the parties concerned should first be sought regarding the Marseille case, and then discussed by the Administrative Council. It is advisable not to continue the discussion before such a solution is reached, as public discussions only cause confusion and are of no help. However, although the three major powers have agreed to proceed in this way, the consent of other members of the Administrative Council must also be obtained, especially Romanian Foreign Minister Titulescu. On the seventh, during the first discussion of the Marseille case by the Administrative Council, Titulescu requested that the reply from Hungary to South Korea's application be submitted for discussion and refuted, and stated that the debate could not be concluded until Hungary's reply was refuted. The Administrative Council, originally scheduled to meet tomorrow morning, has been postponed until the afternoon. In addition, Laval also explained to the representatives of various countries that a good solution must be found in the shortest possible time. If it is delayed indefinitely, people will be disappointed, and the parties concerned will consider the League of Nations unreliable and seek their own solutions. If so, there will be great chaos. At present, security hangs by a thread. A slight carelessness or a momentary misunderstanding in strategy can destroy the peace of Europe. We must be extremely cautious about this. (Havas Telegram, 9th)

(Geneva) – Yesterday, during the meeting of the League of Nations Administrative Council, French Foreign Minister Laval delivered a speech, which was divided into three main points: (1) Some Hungarian government offices are involved in the Marseille murder case and should be held responsible. (2) The Hungarian government should conduct a formal reinvestigation. (3) A draft convention should be studied as soon as possible to define the "right of countries to harbor political prisoners." It is now reported that international sources say that the Yugoslav delegation may be able to accept this draft resolution, but unfortunately, the delegations of Italy and Hungary are opposed to it. It is reported that talks will continue tomorrow. (Reuters Telegram, 9th)

League of Nations Discusses Convention on Punishing Terrorists

Criminals to Be Tried by International Court

(Geneva) – The League of Nations Administrative Council met this afternoon to continue discussing the dispute between Yugoslavia and Hungary. The Chairman, Portuguese representative Vasconcelos, will read out the French government's memorandum, entitled "The Basis for Concluding an International Convention to Punish All Political Acts of Terrorism." All terrorist acts that plot to assassinate heads of state, government leaders, members of political conferences, and attempt to destroy railways, public buildings, and ships must be punished, and it is stipulated that groups that plot or promote such terrorist acts are also subject to punishment. This convention should still follow the methods stipulated in the 1929 international convention on punishing counterfeit currency, and those who violate it will be submitted to the International Criminal Court for trial. The court will have five judges, and will only convene when there is a violation of the convention. In addition, the convention also stipulates the extradition system for criminals, the accuracy and reliability of guaranteed passports and identity certificates, and that contracting states should immediately notify the countries concerned in detail of any information they obtain about the preparation of criminal actions planned to be carried out in foreign territory. The International League of Nations must also advise its member states to allow political assassination crimes to be included in extradition treaties, as the existing extradition treaties do not allow the extradition of political assassination criminals. (Havas Telegram, 10th)

Yugoslavia Will Not Withdraw from the League of Nations

But Will Withdraw Its Ambassador to Hungary

Henderson Awarded Nobel Peace Prize

Angell Receives Previous Award

Oslo – This year's Nobel Peace Prize has been awarded to Henderson, Chairman of the Disarmament Conference, and the previous Peace Prize has been awarded to British writer Angell, for their efforts for disarmament and peace. The Americans Hopper, who won the Medicine Prize, and Pirandello, who won the Literature Prize, were also present at today's award ceremony. However, Woolley, who won the Chemistry Prize, was absent. This year's Physics Prize was not awarded. (National Telegram, 10th)

Oslo – The 1933 and 1934 Nobel Peace Prizes have both been awarded to British people. The 1933 prize, worth about £7,000, was awarded to the well-known writer and speaker Sir Norman Angell, and the 1934 prize was awarded to former Foreign Secretary and current President of the International Disarmament Conference Arthur Henderson. Henderson also received the 1933 Carnegie Peace Prize of more than £2,000. The awards to both men were long expected, so the news did not surprise people. Sir Angell initially engaged in animal husbandry and mining in the western states of the United States, and later entered the press, which earned him international acclaim. From 1929 to 1931, he served as a Labour Party Member of Parliament. In 1931, he was knighted. He has written extensively, mostly on economics and politics. Sir is generally recognized as an economics expert and is known as a political commentator. Henderson has long been a pillar of the Labour Party. In 1934, when MacDonald organized the first Labour government, Henderson was one of MacDonald's confidants and was appointed Foreign Secretary. In 1931, when the current National Unity Government was established, he separated from MacDonald due to disagreements on political views. After the Disarmament Conference was formed, he was elected as its chairman and has served in this position ever since, sparing no effort to promote peace. Henderson initially worked as a moulder at Robert Stephenson & Co.'s factory in Newcastle, and later became a prominent leader in the trade union movement. In 1903, he was elected as a Member of Parliament. (Reuters Telegram, 10th)

Nanjirō Succeeds Hishikari as Commander of the Kwantung Army

(Tokyo) This morning at ten o'clock, General Nanjirō, accompanied by Prime Minister Okada, met with the Emperor at the Palace. The Emperor appointed General Nanjirō as Commander of the Kwantung Army, Ambassador to Manchukuo, and concurrently Governor of the Kwantung Leased Territory. The Japanese military stated that this reshuffle was a routine change. However, it is widely believed that it was caused by the resignation of the head of the Japanese police alliance in Manchukuo in protest against the reform of the Manchukuo organs. General Nanjirō was the Minister of the Army during the September 18th Incident and is considered the main culprit behind the Manchurian Incident. His appointment to this position is attracting special attention from all parties. When the Okada Cabinet was formed, the naval fleet sent representatives to pressure the government to announce the abolition of naval treaties. General Nanjirō cooperated with this faction, abandoning his former conciliatory stance and was even considered as a candidate to succeed as Prime Minister, which aroused the jealousy of senior statesmen. This appointment as Commander is seen as a promotion in name but in reality, a respectful distancing. (Hua Lian News Agency, 10th)

(Tokyo) The reform of the Manchukuo organs has been decided to be implemented within the year. The Army authorities and the government have been considering candidates in recent days. This morning at ten o'clock, General Nanjirō has been appointed as Commander of the Kwantung Army, concurrently Ambassador to Manchukuo, and Governor of the Kwantung Leased Territory. After the implementation of the reform of the Manchukuo organs, the Governor of Kwantung will naturally disappear, so it will become an integration of the Commander of the Kwantung Army and the Ambassador to Manchukuo. It is heard that General Nanjirō will leave Tokyo for his post on the 19th of this month. The Director-General of the Manchurian Affairs Bureau will be concurrently held by Army Minister Hayashi. For the position of Deputy Director-General, the current Director-General of the Resources Bureau, Haruo Matsui, is the most likely candidate. The Army authorities plan to recommend Colonel Kumakichi Harada, the Second Section Chief of the Kwantung Army Headquarters, as the Chief of the General Affairs Section. Furthermore, the Director of the Administrative Affairs Bureau in Manchukuo (i.e., the Director of the Kwantung Bureau) will be sought from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. (Japan United News Agency, 10th)

(Tokyo) The amendment of the Manchurian institutions and other official regulations and imperial ordinances will be consulted with the Privy Council after the Cabinet meeting on the 11th. Seiyūkai Infighting: Three Factions in Opposition

(Tokyo) The 66th Extraordinary Session of Parliament concluded yesterday. This morning at eleven o'clock, a closing ceremony was held in the House of Peers. The Emperor did not attend. Although the Seiyūkai appears calm on the surface, there is extremely complex infighting within. Before the opening of the extraordinary session, the movement for cooperation between the Seiyūkai and the Minseitō did not show any major flaws. However, the way the cadres presented the emergency motions in the Diet was extremely clumsy. The old Seiyūkai faction, which had always maintained a close but not intimate relationship with the Suzuki faction, completely broke away from the Suzuki faction due to emotional incompatibility. This allowed the Tokonami faction to take advantage of the situation. Currently, the actions of the Kuhara faction are most noteworthy. Since the emergence of the Seiyūkai-Minseitō alliance theory, Kuhara has gradually expanded his power, believing that the current motion issue is a scheme by the Hatoyama faction to overthrow Kuhara's power. As a result, the feelings between the two factions have become increasingly bitter. The Seiyūkai is divided into the Suzuki faction, the Kuhara faction, and the old Seiyūkai faction, making it doubtful whether the unification issue can be realized. (Japan United News Agency, 3rd)

Success of German Winter Relief Drive

People Nationwide Generously Contribute

Huge Sum Raised in Five Hours

(Berlin) The only way to celebrate "National Solidarity Day" in Germany today was through a grand street collection for the national winter relief effort. Cabinet ministers, dignitaries from all walks of life, famous stage performers, and movie stars personally carried donation boxes to solicit donations. According to public announcements, the results of today's collection were very satisfactory, totaling 3.5 million marks, mostly from small donations of fifty pfennigs each. This afternoon, Head of State Hitler met with Propaganda Minister Goebbels to hear a report on winter relief donations. Goebbels said that the excellent results of the donations were beyond expectations. People across the country felt personal hardship, so they were willing to contribute generously, raising a huge sum of money. Today's donation time was limited to five hours. Compared to the wealthy days of Germany before the European War, when Zeppelin donations continued for five years, the amount raised today in five hours is more than double the previous amount. This shows that the unity of the people today is far greater than before. Furthermore, by region, Berlin alone obtained 200,000 marks. The largest individual donation was 40,000 marks from the President of the National Bank, Schacht, who stood at the entrance of the stock exchange, and brokers, upon seeing him, generously emptied their pockets. Prussian Prime Minister Göring and Propaganda Minister Goebbels both carried boxes and walked back and forth on Berlin's largest boulevard, collecting a total of 12,000 marks. (Guomin News Agency, 9th)

A committee is being organized to control the prices of Italian exports, but there are currently no restrictions on the import and export of gold. (Reuters News Agency, 9th)

US Launches Major Crackdown, Busting Drug Trafficking Organization

Over 750 Arrested

The US Federal Bureau of Narcotics in Baltimore, Maryland, is currently conducting a nationwide drug roundup, which is proceeding rapidly and is quite astonishing. This roundup is the result of seven years of investigation. In 1927, the US first discovered several large-scale drug trafficking incidents, and investigations have continued since then without interruption. This major roundup began in Baltimore and is being conducted simultaneously in major cities across the country. As a result, over 750 drug traffickers have been arrested, including 178 women. By location, 20 were arrested in Boston, 34 in New York, 30 in Philadelphia, 31 in Baltimore, 24 in Atlanta, 43 in New Orleans, 37 in Nashville, 45 in Detroit, 200 in Chicago, 61 in Minneapolis, 117 in Kansas City, 41 in San Antonio, 10 in Denver, 19 in Seattle, and 43 in San Francisco. The police seized the codes used by drug traffickers, thus uncovering the trafficking organization. The codes referred to heroin as "white robes" and opium as "black robes." The drug trafficking organization sold narcotics for $80 per ounce. The police seized a large amount of narcotics, the total value of which is still unknown. (Havas News Agency, 9th)

(Washington) Government troops and police are currently searching for drug traffickers. As of today, a total of 765 people have been arrested, mostly small vendors. Many major criminals are still at large. According to the troops and police, the courts impose very light penalties on addicts, making it difficult to achieve the goal of eradication. These fines are sometimes paid by drug trafficking groups, who view this payment as merely a type of business tax. (Reuters News Agency, 10th)

Australian Aviator Buried in the Pacific Ocean

Search Warships Return to Origin

Honolulu: Australian aviator Ulm and two companions were flying from Oakland, California, to Australia. While flying near Honolulu, they encountered danger and landed in the sea, sending out a distress radio message. French Divorce Statistics for Fifty Years

(Paris) It has been fifty years since France implemented the divorce law. According to statistics from the Ministry of Justice, French courts have approved a total of 722,866 divorces during these fifty years. The various details are as follows:

(1) Couples are most likely to be involved in divorce in the first five years.

(2) More often, the wife petitions for divorce than the husband.

(3) Cruelty is the leading cause of divorce, followed by adultery.

(4) Paris is no longer a place for English and American women to divorce.

(5) Divorce in France is increasing day by day, but it was temporarily suspended during the European War.

The French divorce law was formally promulgated in July 1884 and implemented in September of that year. Within a few months, 1,657 divorce cases were established. In 1885, it increased to 4,123 cases. In 1887, it increased to 5,797 cases. In 1912, it reached 16,723 cases. However, during the European War, divorce cases decreased significantly, with only 1,952 cases in 1915. But in 1919, it surged again to 19,465 cases. Since then, it has increased without decreasing, reaching 28,505 cases in 1931. Looking at the statistics for the past fifty years, Paris, the most prosperous city in the world, also has the most prevalent divorce. (Guomin News Agency, 10th)

Capital Enforces Strict Ban on Opium

Significance of the Anti-Opium Campaign Week

(Nanjing) On the morning of the 10th, at the Capital City Government Memorial Week, Secretary-General Lai Lian reported on the opium ban issue in the capital, saying that the temporary opium addiction treatment hospitals established by the City Government have been established in four locations within three days, from the 7th to the 9th: (1) Municipal Opium Addiction Treatment Hospital, (2) Hubei Branch of the Gulou Health Office, (3) Municipal Infectious Disease Hospital, (4) New Building of the Dengfushan Relief Home. (Nanjing) An official of the Anti-Opium Association estimates that there are approximately 7,000 opium addicts in the capital, accounting for only 1% of the total population. Compared with the opium-smoking elements in Sichuan and Yunnan, this is still a small number, making it easier to eradicate. Regarding the issue of punishing opium addicts, because opium addicts have already become useless people, it is not impossible to impose capital punishment. However, because of the large number of people, we cannot bear to punish them without educating them. Therefore, it has been decided to first use coercive methods to order them to quit in order to open the way for rehabilitation. If they are found to relapse after rehabilitation, the City Government will have stricter sanctions. The methods are currently under discussion. (Special Dispatch, 10th)

(Nanjing) The capital will strictly enforce the opium ban and hold an Anti-Opium Campaign Week. The New Life Movement City Party Headquarters and the City Government will discuss the implementation measures within days. (Central News Agency, 10th)

(Nanjing) The capital has organized a Committee for Eradicating Opium and established temporary opium addiction treatment hospitals, etc. The estimated cost is 100,000 yuan. Kong Xiangxi, the director of the fundraising group, has promised to allocate funds from the Ministry of Finance immediately. (Special Dispatch, 10th)

Anglo-Polish Trade Agreement Negotiations

Warsaw Special Dispatch: Poland is currently in a period of intense commercial negotiations. Talks on concluding new commercial agreements with many countries have resumed. The first to resume were the Anglo-Polish trade agreement negotiations. The United Kingdom occupies a very important position in Poland's foreign trade. In the past year, the goods purchased by the United Kingdom from Poland were worth 15 million Polish zlotys, or 19.2% of Poland's total exports. Germany ranked second with 17.5%, and Austria ranked third with 5.8%. The importance of the United Kingdom in Poland's foreign trade has an important economic impact on the current negotiations. The recent increase in British investment in the Polish market has a significant influence on these negotiations. Between 1931 and 1934, Poland concluded three loans with the United Kingdom, namely the telephone loan in 1931 and the railway loans in 1933 and 1934. Comparatively, the amount of these loans increased each time, while the interest rate gradually decreased. The 1931 loan was £550,000 with an interest rate of 6.2%. The 1933 loan reached £2,000,000 with an interest rate of 6.4%. The 1934 loan reached £5,000,000 with an interest rate of 6.5%. In addition, British capital has also been invested in other Polish industries, such as sugar, timber, insurance, and banking. Poland is a debtor country to the United Kingdom. At the same time, it buys less from the United Kingdom than the United Kingdom buys from it. Therefore, its debt can be compensated by its trade surplus, so the United Kingdom can better understand the soundness of the Polish economy, because its goods transported to the creditor country are sufficient to offset its debts to that creditor country. This opinion is recognized by the most influential politicians and economists in the United Kingdom. Although some British people have doubts about the existing Anglo-Polish relations, Poland's trade surplus with the United Kingdom should receive good attention in this trade agreement negotiation.

Public Security Team Cooperating with Local Militia to Intercept

(Tianjin) Suddenly, on the 9th, over 300 bandits were discovered in the Yiyuan Pass and Chengziyu areas of Linyu County. They were fully armed and carried several machine guns, claiming that they would attack the pass to find food. People from all walks of life in Shimenzhai and near the Liujiang Coal Mine were extremely panicked. Yao Zhendong, the Captain of the Public Security Team of Shanhaiguan, has led a team of hundreds of people to cooperate with the local militia to intercept them and has deployed defenses along the border wall. (Special Dispatch, 10th)

Four Japanese Destroyers Arrive at Qinhuangdao

(Tianjin) Four ships of the Japanese Third Fleet Destroyer Squadron 26, including the Kuri, arrived at Qinhuangdao from Lushun on the morning of the 9th and docked outside the small pier. Sailors landed and toured, and some officers went to Haiyangzhen to survey the terrain. They sailed to Zhifu early on the 10th. (Special Dispatch, 10th)

Continued Arrests of Remaining Members of the Fake Anti-Japanese Army in Jinan

(Jinan) Zhu Zhentang and others, who were members of the fake "People's Anti-Japanese Salvation Army" and were arrested in Jinan this autumn, have been sentenced to imprisonment. At that time, Han Dianjiang reported to Chiang Kai-shek, who praised him and ordered the continued arrest of the remaining members. Recently, the fake Commander-in-Chief You Renxiao has set up an organization at No. 14 Tushan Street in the commercial district, still using the name Yimin Company, and using stocks as commissions. For example, 10,000 yuan worth of stocks represented a division commander, and 5,000 yuan represented a brigade commander. The Special Detective Team learned of this and arrested the fake division commander Wang Shude early this morning, seizing many stocks. Wang confessed that there were also Chief of Staff Fa Ziheng and his son Fa Yi, who were operating at the Tie Gong Temple by Daming Lake. They were also arrested. Fa then confessed that You Renxiao's representatives Wang Zhenqiu, Ding Juzheng, and Wang Shude's commissioned recruiters Wu Huchen were also arrested. Subsequently, their party members Sun Chuanxiang and Kang Youtian were arrested in the new market in the commercial district. According to their confession, apart from the fake representative Ren Tianzhu, who returned to his native Hejian, the rest have been rounded up. They are now detained at the Military Law Office. (Special Dispatch, 10th)

Wuhan Police Department Stipulates Measures to Protect Japanese Residents

(Hankou) The Wuhan Police Department has stipulated four measures to protect Japanese residents and sent a letter to the Japanese Consul for reference on the 10th. When Japanese residents, officials, or public organizations go outside the Japanese concession, they must notify the police in advance to send officers to accompany them for proper protection. (Special Dispatch, 10th)

Anhui Provincial Government Borrows Money from Five Banks

Contract Signed Yesterday in Wuhu

(Wuhu) The Anhui Provincial Government borrowed 1.2 million yuan from five banks, including the Central Bank. The contract was signed in Wuhu on the 10th. 800,000 yuan will be paid within the year, and the rest will be paid next spring. (Special Dispatch, 10th)

Guangdong Railway Trains Collide

(Hong Kong) At 8:30 this morning, the first passenger train heading south from Xinshi on the Guangdong Railway collided with a northbound train at Xicun Station, injuring the driver and 28 passengers. (Special Dispatch, 10th)

(Xiamen) The Xiamen Overseas Chinese Affairs Bureau was established on the 10th, located on Shengping Road, and divided into three sections: General Affairs, Guidance, and Social Affairs. (Special Dispatch, 10th)

(Nanjing) The 190th routine meeting of the Executive Yuan was originally scheduled to be held on the morning of the 11th. Because Premier Wang and the ministers of various ministries will all attend the opening of the Fifth Plenary Session of the Kuomintang Central Committee, it has been changed to this afternoon. It is heard that the issue of reorganizing the Zhejiang Provincial Government will be discussed. (Special Dispatch, 10th)

Shao Lizi Sends Telegram Congratulating Li Zongren's Troops on Their Victory in Suppressing Bandits

(Nanjing) Shao Lizi, Chairman of Shaanxi Province, came to Nanjing to attend the Fifth Plenary Session of the Kuomintang Central Committee. He received a telegram from Li Zongren reporting victory in bandit suppression. Shao immediately replied by telegram, saying: "To Commander-in-Chief Li Delin of Nanning, I am delighted to learn from your telegram that your troops have repeatedly achieved victories in blocking and attacking the remaining bandits. The long-standing bandit disaster has been declared eradicated. Your extraordinary achievements are celebrated throughout the country. I send you this telegram to express my congratulations and wish you continued success." (Special Dispatch, 10th)

(Guangzhou) The Guilin Headquarters of the Guangxi Army telegraphed today that after fierce fighting between the Guangxi Army and the Communists in the Xing'an area on the border of Guangxi and Guizhou, 3,000 Communist bandits were captured. It also stated that the Communist bandits who fled west from Jiangxi Province originally numbered over 70,000, and now only 40,000 remain. These bandits are still planning to enter Sichuan through Guizhou. (Reuters News Agency, 10th)

Guangzhou Chamber of Commerce Asks for Release of Guangdong Rice Seized by the Jianghai Customs

(Nanjing) The Guangzhou Chamber of Commerce submitted a petition to the Executive Yuan stating that Guangdong Province suffered a drought this year and lacked food. In order to regulate the people's food supply, Guangdong local rice was transported to Shanghai for sale to purchase wheat for regulation. After arriving in Shanghai, it was seized by the Jianghai Customs, which not only hinders the people's food supply but is also detrimental to farmers and merchants. They earnestly request that an order be issued for immediate release. The Executive Yuan has instructed the Ministry of Finance to investigate and handle the matter. (Special Dispatch, 10th)

International Business Telegraph

-Special Commercial Telegram of Reuters News Agency on December 10-

Gold and Silver

The price of gold in London today (the 10th) has fallen by three and a half pence to 140 shillings and four and a half pence.

The price of silver in London today (the 10th) fell by one and two fifths at the opening. The spot price is 24 and a half pence, and the futures price is 24 and six two fifths. India and China sold in the morning, while speculators bought when the price fell. The market is calm.

The price of silver in the Mount Lyell silver market today is slightly lower, and the transaction is also sluggish.

Exchange Rate

The foreign exchange market in London, England and the United States was stable this morning. The opening price of the exchange rate between England and the United States was four dollars, nine corners and four and seventy-five cents, which was one two fifths higher than the closing price between the United States and England on Saturday. At noon, it rose five six two fifths, reaching four dollars, nine corners and five and three one two fifths cents, then fell back one two fifths to four dollars, nine corners and five and one eighth fifths cents, which is the latest price. Also, one US dollar equals four shillings and zero four six six pence of English gold.

The opening price between England and France rose by six pounds. At eleven o'clock, it rose by another six pounds, reaching 75 francs 15. Then it stabilized until the power was turned off. There was no change in this price.

In the foreign exchange market in New York, United States, the opening price of the exchange rate between the United States and England was four dollars, nine corners and five and twenty-five cents, which was six two fifths higher than the previous closing price. Later, the pound sterling weakened, and the price was four dollars, nine corners and four and eighty-seven fifths cents, which was three seventh fifths lower than the opening price.

Cotton and Wheat

American Cotton: The cotton market opened steadily today. Liverpool bought, and retail investors sold slightly. The market price rose slightly, but generally speaking, the market situation was very sluggish. The 1935 government cotton program roughly does not include loans, so that surplus cotton can compete in export trade.

American Wheat: The wheat market trend is looser.

English Cotton: The Liverpool cotton market was quiet this morning. At one o'clock in the afternoon, the price for May was 6.68, which was the same as the price on Sunday.

English Wheat: The Liverpool wheat market was also quiet today. The May futures price did not move and remained at five shillings and pence six two fifths.

Rubber

The market situation in London this morning was calm. At noon, the transaction price for April 6th was six pence five sixth fifths, which was 0 sixth fifths lower than the closing price on Saturday.

The rubber market in New York today (the 10th) is sluggish, and there are not many transactions.

Securities

Before the opening of the New York Stock Exchange today (the 10th), the factors favorable to the market situation were: (1) According to the steel industry report, the working hours of steel mills last week increased to 30% of their productivity, and there is a sign of continued increase; (2) The sales volume of General Motors in November is satisfactory; (3) There is no sign of a major reaction; (4) The rise in some stocks is expected to resume soon. The unfavorable factor in the market situation is that the political situation in Europe is uneasy, making people wary. The stock market opened today, and the market situation was slightly active. The prices were mixed, but the fluctuations were limited to zero. Merchants are still waiting for new impetus. It is expected that there will be no major development in the market situation. The stock market prices in New York are listed on the left.

Economic Commission Plans Shaanxi-Gansu-Sichuan Liaison Highway

(Nanjing) Regarding the Shaanxi-Gansu-Sichuan liaison highway, the Economic Commission has prepared a plan to change the route of the Gansu-Sichuan highway planned to be built by Gansu Province, connect it with the Xi'an-Han Road in Shaanxi Province in Lueyang, and then go from Lueyang through Ningqiang to Guangyuan in Sichuan. The Association has sent letters to the Shaanxi and Gansu provincial governments to solicit opinions. Considering that the road has considerable military value and is of great importance to the transportation of the three provinces of Shaanxi, Gansu, and Sichuan, the Association sent a surveying team to survey the route. The work began at the beginning of this month. The Economic Commission is responsible for 40% of the construction costs, and Gansu Province is responsible for 60%. If the route is decided to pass through Shaanxi Province, the remaining 60% will be shared by Shaanxi and Gansu provinces. (Special dispatch on the 10th)

Strict Eradication of Opium Seedlings in Huian, Southern Fujian

Troops Ordered to Go to the Countryside to Supervise the Eradication

Jinjiang County Will Also Eradicate Opium Seedlings

Xiamen Correspondence, the people of Huian County in southern Fujian have privately planted tens of thousands of acres of opium. After the provincial government found out, it strictly ordered the Quanzhou-based Southern Fujian Bandit Suppression Headquarters and the Huian County magistrate to jointly and severely eradicate it. Xiao Jing, the bandit suppression commander, and Yang Yu, the Huian County magistrate, immediately issued a notice to the people, setting a deadline for automatic eradication. Those who failed to do so would be sent to the countryside to supervise the eradication. Those who replant after eradication will be sentenced to death, and the township chiefs will be held jointly liable. After the notice was issued, many people were still watching. Therefore, the county government joined forces with the garrison troops to go to the countryside to supervise the eradication. According to the Huian News, the Chen Security Group was ordered to supervise the eradication of opium seedlings. The group left a platoon in Tuling, and the rest all went to the Batou area on November 18. They went to the countryside every day to supervise the eradication. On the 18th, villagers in the areas of Zhongcuo, Shanyao, Batou, Fengwei, Guocuo, Sanchen, Shi Wu Wang, Tukeng, Xiao Cuo, and Xialupai saw the troops going to the countryside and automatically eradicated them. There were no less than 20,000 acres of opium seedlings in the Batou area. The supervision of the eradication took ten days to complete. The group is currently leaving the ninth company under Xu Yubu stationed in Batou for supervision. The rest will then open up the Tuling and Wangchuan areas. On November 27, they went to various townships near Tuling to supervise the eradication. The townships of Sanxiang and Huangtian in the area, relying on their high mountains and mountains, and the townships of Hongcuo, Kengqian, Ouhengxi, and Dashe, because they were located in the mountains, did not eradicate them in the end. The eighth company of the Chen regiment arrived in Sanxiang on the 29th, and the sixth company arrived in Yiban. They all implemented the supervision of the eradication. However, the Wangchuan area was originally close to the county seat. When the troops went to the countryside, not only did they not eradicate them, but they continued to sow them. On the 29th, the Chen regiment sent the third company and the seventh company and convened a meeting of the township chiefs of the Wangchuan area, declaring that they were ordered to strictly enforce them and must not disobey the crime. Currently, the townships of Fengqi, Xudai, Wangchuan, Shekeng, Houkeng, Xishan, Xifu, Nanzhuang, Tapu, Liuxia, Chuicuo, Ganlu, Qianyang, Houpan, Dongcun, Sheba, Xiashe, Weitoukeng, Nanku, Xiazhuang, Houxu, Wangsha, Nanwei, Qianxing, and Xiwei have all been more than half eradicated. Also, the Dongling and Tuzhai areas, which are located in eastern Huian, have started the eradication of opium in northern Huian first. Therefore, the troops have not yet gone to the various townships in the two areas. Generally, after the Wangchuan and Tuling areas are eradicated, troops will be sent to them. The Huangtang area is located in western Huian and is connected to Tianchuan. It was once occupied by the bandits Wang Lianming, Wang Hanmin, and Wang Yunlong, who have been executed. It has always been called the bandit lair. The people do not fear the law. Since the Republic of China, poisonous flowers have been everywhere for many years. On December 3, the Chen regiment sent the fourth company to the area to start supervising the eradication. Chen Peiyu, the head of the regiment, also personally went to the area on the 5th to convene a meeting of township chiefs, preparing to eradicate them all within half a month. This is the current situation of the eradication of opium in Huian. In addition to the large-scale private planting of opium by the villagers in Huian, opium seedlings were also found in the Jinjiang County Golden Well Stone Lion townships. The Jinjiang County magistrate summoned the chiefs of each district and strictly ordered them to be eradicated automatically within a time limit. If they failed to do so, troops would be sent to the countryside to supervise the eradication. (December 8)

The Pizhou Bandits Fled to Southern Shandong

The Remaining Bandits Are Trapped in Guozhuang

The Police and Group Strictly Defend Northern Pizhou

Xuzhou Correspondence, Pizhou is located in the northeast of Xuzhou and is adjacent to Shandong Province. When the Liu Guitang bandit force disturbed Lidong, the 7th Division troops had set up defenses in northern Pizhou. Later, the Liu bandits fled north, the troops were demobilized, and the local bandits joined forces and gradually formed a large force. Also, because the land is located on the border of northern Jiangsu and borders southern Shandong, it is easy for roaming bandits to secretly multiply. Wang Depu, the administrative inspector and security commander of the Tongshan District, felt that the Pizhou bandits were rampant during his inspection of eastern Xuzhou this time, so he launched a large-scale suppression. In addition to transferring the Tongshan and Suining County security teams to Pizhou to cooperate in the suppression with the Pizhou County security team, he also telegraphed to transfer a battalion of the first regiment of the provincial security team stationed in Suqian to Pizhou, concentrated their forces, and added temporary organization. Wang sat in Pizhou County to supervise the suppression and organized a bandit suppression cooperation association, offering rewards for the arrest of bandit leaders, and setting a deadline for clearing the Sutangying area in the third district of southern Pizhou and Xiaoliuzhuang and Guozhuang, where there are large bandit gangs of about 100 people. Each team attacked together, first defeating the bandits in Sutangying, and then trapping the remaining bandits in Guozhuang. They abandoned the village at night and fled across the water. Each team pursued and killed many hostages. The Tongshan and Suining security teams returned to defense, and the provincial security team remained in southern Pizhou for defense. Currently, civil self-defense forces are being organized. Wang presented Qin Jieren, the magistrate of Suining County, for his outstanding performance in handling Baojia, to the province to be transferred with Fei Gongxia, the magistrate of Pizhou County, and ordered that residents in each Bao who have guns should be organized into a detachment, with the Bao chief concurrently serving as the detachment leader. Each township will form a regiment, with the township chief concurrently serving as the regiment leader. Each district will form a squadron, with the district chief concurrently serving as the squadron leader. The county magistrate will concurrently serve as the squadron leader of the entire county. After the organization is completed, simple military training will be carried out. After the bandits in southern Pizhou are resolved, the police and group forces of Pizhou County will set out to attack. Most of the bandits have fled to Yixian, Yishui, and Tancheng in southern Shandong. Wang then telegraphed Han Fuju, the chairman of Shandong Province, to request cooperation in the suppression. Han telegraphed back saying that he had ordered the Li Brigade stationed in southern Shandong to intercept them. Currently, northern Pizhou is also defended by the police and group to prepare for a pincer attack. Wang returned to Xuzhou yesterday, leaving Chief of Staff Li Fuzhen in Pizhou to command. After the affairs in Xuzhou are completed, he will go to Pizhou for inspection to complete the local self-defense force and prevent bandit troubles from growing again. (9th)

Guangzhou City West Fire

The Ruyi Fang Market Reduced to Ashes

More Than One Hundred and Fifty Shops Burned Down

Guangzhou Correspondence: The Ruyi Fang in Huangsha, Guangzhou City, located in the west of the city, is a prosperous commercial area. However, as it has not yet been developed into a proper road, the shops are densely packed side by side. Recently, with high winds and dry conditions, a fire broke out at the Xiang Zhan ironware and general merchandise store, number 140 on the street, at 2:20 AM on the 2nd of this month, due to carelessly discarded embers behind the shop, causing a conflagration. That night, a fierce north wind was blowing, and the wind fueled the flames, quickly turning it into a raging fire. Firefighters from all over the city rushed to put out the fire. However, due to the narrow streets, fire trucks could not get close, and could only pump water from the river and spray from a distance. As a result, the fire raged fiercely. Furthermore, the buildings of the shops were mostly made of wood, which easily caught fire, making it even more difficult to extinguish. The fire brigade tore down structures to create firebreaks to contain the flames, while also rescuing residents from danger. At that time, the red glow lit up the sky, and the cries of people filled the air, creating a truly tragic scene. The fire spread so widely that it was impossible to approach. The small fire trucks were like a drop in the bucket, unable to make a difference. Later, firefighting ships on the river used hoses to pump water and fight the fire. After four hours of chaos, the flames were finally extinguished at 6:00 AM. However, the entire Ruyi Fang market had been reduced to ashes, with more than one hundred and fifty shops burned down. Several dozen boat dwellers' shacks were also burned, and seventy or eighty boats along the shore were destroyed by the fire. An investigation revealed that the burned shops included numbers 52 to 162 (even numbers) on Huangsha police district, a total of 57 shops; and numbers 45 to 159 (odd numbers), a total of 58 shops; plus 7 shops with additional numbers, totaling 121 shops. Among them, 89 were stores, 14 were residential units, and 1 was a public place. In the E Tan police district, 31 shops were affected by the fire. In total, the two districts had 152 shops affected by the fire. During the fire, an elderly boat woman drowned while trying to escape the flames. On land, no less than four or five hundred shopkeepers and refugees were affected, with more than a hundred people left homeless, shivering in the cold, snowy night. The next day, charities in the city purchased cotton clothing and food to distribute to the victims. (December 3rd)

Taixian County's Unauthorized Levy of Field Tax for Guiding the Huai River

County Residents Petition the Provincial Government to Stop It

The Jiangsu Provincial Government issued a general order to all counties in the Huai River region to mobilize labor for guiding the Huai River, originally stipulating that no wages would be paid, but that laborers would receive eight cents for food per cubic meter of earth moved. As such, each county obeyed the province's order. Zhang Yi, the magistrate of Taixian County and concurrently the chairman of the Taixian County Guidance of the Huai River Labor Mobilization Assistance Committee, believed that the provincial rate of eight cents per cubic meter was too low. He decided that, in addition to the eight cents provided by the province, the local government would add another fifteen cents in wages, requiring approximately 157,500 yuan. Including the committee's operating expenses, the total cost was estimated to be around 200,000 yuan. He issued a public notice to levy a field tax per mu. The residents of the county believed that levying a field tax without requesting approval from the provincial departments violated Sun Yat-sen's principle of "voluntary labor," Chiang Kai-shek's principle that "the people have an obligation to serve the public every year," and the policy of the Huai River Guidance Committee on labor mobilization. Recently, it was heard that local gentry Huang Tong had been publicly elected to separately submit petitions to the provincial government's finance department, requesting that it be stopped.

Suzhou

Nine Robbery Suspects Escorted to Zhenjiang for Trial

The case of the armed robbery at the home of Zhou Dongwen, a well-known insurance businessman (i.e., Yongming Life Insurance Company) on Xiatang Street in Changmen, Suzhou, resulted in the arrest of nine male and female suspects, including Qian Dehua. Zhang Yilin, a local resident, had sent a telegram to the provincial authorities, requesting that they be severely punished according to the law to quell the atmosphere of robbery. The county government also considered the case to be extremely serious, as it occurred in an area with numerous military police. It planned to handle the case according to military law and submitted a request to the province for instructions. Now, the county government has received approval from the province to escort all suspects and witnesses to the Zhenjiang Garrison Headquarters for trial at 1:00 AM on the 10th.

Villagers Repel Lake Bandits

Four or five li southeast of Xiangcheng, at 11:00 PM on the night of the 9th, twenty or thirty lake bandits landed from the Yangcheng Lake area, carrying torches and weapons, and swarmed towards nearby villages, intending to rob them. Villagers spotted the torchlight and immediately beat gongs to gather a crowd. They used muskets to shoot down one bandit. Fan Hao, the leader of the 2nd Security Brigade stationed in the town, also heard the alarm and led his team to the scene. The remaining bandits, seeing the situation was unfavorable, began to flee. The wounded bandit was captured. On the morning of the 10th, he was taken to the city. He was identified as Xu Jingaog, but claimed he felt unwell, and he had been injured on the head. He was said to be very dangerous and needed to be sent to the hospital for treatment before being interrogated.

Kunshan

Thugs Murder and Commit Arson in the Middle of the Night

In Hongjiatan Village, Bacheng Township, Kunshan County, there lived an elderly Henan woman named Zhu, in her sixties, and her son, Minghai, who had been renting and farming land there for more than ten years. Their lives were generally comfortable. Unexpectedly, the night before last, in the middle of the night, Gao Laowu and Gao Beiquan from Tongzhou in the neighboring village, along with several others, broke down their door, ransacked the house, and tied up and beat Zhu and her son. Zhu, who was old, was strangled to death. Not satisfied, the thugs set the house on fire, and the three rooms were quickly consumed. At the time of the fire, Minghai was tied up but managed to struggle free and escape. Zhu's body was burned into charcoal and was difficult to identify. Afterwards, the township chief, Qian Wosheng, reported the incident to the Fifth Public Security Sub-Bureau. Sub-Bureau Chief Bao dispatched police to arrest the perpetrators, Gao Laowu and Gao Beiquan. Yesterday, they were escorted to the county government and taken into custody. In the afternoon, examiner Zhang, along with a coroner, went to the scene to conduct an autopsy. The victim, Zhu Minghai, sustained serious injuries and is currently receiving treatment at Kunshan Hospital. It is said that his life is in danger.

Wuxi

Bean Trade Restores 99 Discount

The Wuxi Rice and Bean Merchants Association, due to the declining grain prices and the increasing burden of taxes and expenses last year, found that the original 99 discount was insufficient to sustain their operations. They specially changed it to 98.4, which caused a strong backlash from grain merchants in Bengbu. Through the mediation of the Chamber of Commerce, the rate was changed from 98.4 to 98.6, with the stipulation that if the price of miscellaneous grains and beans exceeded five yuan, the 99 discount would be restored. Merchants in Wuxi and Changzhou uniformly complied. Recently, bean merchants in Bengbu, seeing that the market price of soybeans had gradually increased and had long exceeded five yuan, sent a letter through the Chamber of Commerce to the Rice and Bean Merchants Association, requesting that the original agreement be upheld and the 99 discount be restored. Upon receiving the notification, the Rice and Bean Merchants Association immediately convened a meeting of its members and obtained the consent of the Wujin Bean Trade. It was decided that, starting from January 1, 1935, the 99 discount would be restored, but only for Bengbu beans from the north and south rivers. The other bean varieties would not be included.

Younger Brother Killed by Older Brother; Perpetrator Arrested

Wang Quanbao, a fisherman living in a boat under the awning outside the West Gate, in front of the Fifth Fire Brigade, had an argument with his older brother, Wang Quansheng, last month due to a business dispute, which led to a fight. Quanbao was severely injured and died the next day. Quansheng, realizing he had caused a disaster, fled to escape punishment. The local branch of the court sent a letter to the county government, ordering the public security organs on land and water and all local militias to arrest him. Yesterday morning around 8:00 AM, Zhong Jihe, the captain of the Public Security Bureau's detective team, learned that the perpetrator, Wang Quansheng, was planning to take a Jiangnan bus to Yixing to hide. He immediately dispatched detectives Hua Bingquan and Gao Lin to the bus station, where they arrested the suspect and brought him back to the bureau for temporary detention, pending transfer to the local branch of the court for trial.

Changzhou

Drug Dealer Wu Zhongquan Executed by Firing Squad

Wu Zhongquan, a drug dealer, was previously arrested by the Wu County government and escorted to the Zhenjiang Garrison Headquarters for trial. He was sentenced to death, and the verdict was approved by the Nanchang Headquarters and sent back to the original county for execution. Upon receiving the order, Magistrate Hou immediately dispatched police to sign for the prisoner this morning (the 10th) at 10:00 AM, verified his identity, tied him up, and executed him by firing squad at the Fengweidun execution ground.

Local News

Celebration Rally Held Yesterday in Shanghai by Various Circles for the Victory Over the Bandits and the Opening of the Fifth Plenary Session

More than 3,000 People Attended the Meeting at the Chamber of Commerce in the Morning

Flags Were Hung Throughout the City, and Airplanes Scattered Leaflets in the Sky

Over a Hundred Cars and Five Ships Paraded on Land and Sea

According to the Central News Agency, the Shanghai representatives' celebration rally for the victory over the bandits was held at 10:00 a.m. yesterday in the auditorium of the Chamber of Commerce at Tianhou Temple Bridge. A car parade was held in the afternoon, and representatives from all walks of life attended. The details are recorded as follows:

Representatives Attending The representatives who attended yesterday's celebration rally included: Chen Kecheng from the Municipal Government, Xing Wan from the Municipal Party Headquarters, Tao Baichuan from the Songhu Garrison Headquarters, Tian Heqing from the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, Xu Zeye from the Municipal Education Association, Yu Zhenhui from the Municipal Farmers' Association, Yu Zuoting from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Huang Hanliang from the First Special District Citizens' Federation, Mao Yun from the Second Special District Citizens' Federation, Lin Kecong from the Municipal Women's Association, as well as over 3,000 representatives from various trade associations, labor unions, schools at all levels, and party and government organizations.

Xing's Report After the ceremony, Xing Wan of the presidium first delivered a report, stating in brief: Since unifying China, the Chinese Nationalist Party should have had ample opportunity for national and social construction. However, the circumstances at the time made it difficult to fulfill this wish. The root cause was the occupation by the communist bandits, which was a major obstacle. The Party took action to separate from the communists around 1928 because the communist party not only undermined our Party but also the country. Since the separation, the communist bandits first launched a major riot in Guangdong, then fled to Jiangxi, using it as their base for rebellion. At that time, the communist bandit scourge extended to nearly seven or eight provinces. The central government, facing foreign invasion and internal strife, although it mobilized a large army for encirclement and suppression, could not achieve immediate results. It was in this difficult situation that Chairman Chiang personally visited the front lines, supervised the soldiers, and won the support of the people, leading to today's unprecedented victory over the bandits. From this, we have learned (1) that nothing is impossible under the heavens, it only depends on our efforts and struggles. Today, disregarding all difficulties, we fight to the end with the spirit of revolution and have achieved this victory, which proves that the Three Principles of the People will surely triumph. The communist party in China is very different from the communist party in Soviet Russia. The communist party in Soviet Russia is still based on the nation and ethnicity, while the communist party in China is merely a peasant uprising from the feudal era. (2) If we do things based on the spirits of loyalty, filial piety, benevolence, love, faith, righteousness, and peace, we can accomplish anything. Now that the red bandits in Jiangxi have been defeated and the remaining bandits will soon be eliminated, from today onwards, the first stage can be considered complete and the second stage will continue to begin. The focus of the work in the second stage should be on production and construction. Production and construction should have the following preconditions: (1) The entire nation should unite with sincerity. The so-called sincere unity is different from the cooperation that people generally talk about today. Since we are all comrades of the same party and compatriots of the same country, we should cooperate with each other. (2) Implement the recent telegram between Mr. Wang and Mr. Chiang to achieve balanced power. The power of balanced power is the power to handle affairs. In other words, the personnel of local governments should be truly responsible. It does not mean that with the implementation of balanced power, local areas can freely handle everything and govern themselves. Therefore, in the future, if anyone deviates from the original intention of balanced power, they should be suppressed with the spirit of defeating the bandits in the past. (3) Production and construction must require the people of the whole country to abide by order and discipline. The so-called abiding by order and discipline must also be imbued with the spirit of loyalty, filial piety, benevolence, love, faith, righteousness, and peace. If so, the future of the country will surely be bright and full of hope.

Tao's Speech Tao Baichuan then delivered a speech, briefly stating: Comrade Xing has reported in great detail on the significance of celebrating the victory over the bandits. However, I would like to add a few points to Comrade Xing's remarks on the points of effort for the future. Although the red bandits in Jiangxi and Fujian have been defeated today, these fellows still have 100,000 men and 30,000 guns, and have fled to places like Sichuan and Guizhou. With Sichuan's treacherous terrain and abundant resources, I fear they will still cause trouble in the future. In the past, the red bandits had two routes: one was the international route, and the other was the Luo Ming route. In the past, the Third International sent the Indian Luo Ming to China for secret investigation. After returning, he made suggestions to the Third International. He believed that the Chinese red bandits in Jiangxi and Fujian were easily blockaded by the Party's military fortresses and highways to their death, so they should flee from Fujian and Jiangxi to Sichuan, and then hope to seize Shaanxi or Gansu, so as to connect with Inner and Outer Mongolia, so that the Red Army of Soviet Russia could be contacted at any time. This is the so-called Luo Ming route. However, the Third International did not adopt it. The Third International believed that the Chinese red revolution had reached the stage of maturity, so it should develop towards the Yangtze River and Pearl River basins and seek to seize cities. This is the so-called international route. There was a fierce debate between these two routes in the Chinese Communist Party. Now, the international route has been defeated by the central government's policies of highway fortresses and blockades. Therefore, these fellows may engage in the Luo Ming route. Therefore, we should intensify our work in the future, taking advantage of the red bandits being newly wounded, and the Party's army can take advantage of the victory to pursue them to seek thorough elimination. In addition, regarding the work of continuing to suppress the bandits, military force only accounts for three parts, while politics accounts for seven parts. This is the experience that Chairman Chiang has gained over the years, and he has set this grand plan. In the past year, the work of suppressing bandits in Jiangxi and Fujian has followed this spirit, so there is today's victory. Furthermore, peace and unity are indeed important for China today. Although this statement has become a cliché, it is actually very important and should not be ignored. In the past, the reason why suppressing bandits did not win victory was because the internal chaos had not been extinguished. Today, the country is relatively peaceful and relatively unified, so it can achieve unprecedented victory in suppressing bandits. After the victory over the bandits, attention should be paid to the completion of local autonomy. The important tasks of local autonomy are education, nurturing, and defense. Educate the people so that everyone has knowledge; nurture the people so that everyone can live and work in peace; and protect the people so that everyone has armed force. If so, the country will be prosperous and the people will be safe, and the people will not be exploited by the red bandits, and the nation can rely on it to revive. There was also a speech by Lin Kecong, which was lengthy and will be omitted.

The telegrams are recorded as follows: (1) Telegram to comfort Chairman Chiang and the bandit suppression generals and soldiers said: The red bandits have been rampant for many years, harming the Party and the country, and poisoning the people. The disasters they caused were even more severe than those of Chuang and Xian. Fortunately, you supervised the army to suppress them severely, and the generals and soldiers bravely killed the bandits. As a result, the poisonous atmosphere was swept away and the people were rescued from fire and water. The news of the victory has spread, and the sea is rejoicing. The foundation for the revival of our Chinese nation has been laid here. We hope that you will strictly order the front-line generals and soldiers to take advantage of the victory and drive straight ahead, thoroughly eliminate the remaining evils, and avoid future troubles. This is our sincere comfort.

This is a good opportunity for our nation to recover from the extreme. Your conference is convened at this time to hold a plenary meeting to discuss and plan for internal peace, external resistance, unified construction, and to comfort the people's hope. This is our sincere telegram of congratulations.

Complete Autonomy (3) Please ask the Central Government to eradicate local bullies and complete local autonomy, said: (Title omitted) The red bandits have been rampant for many years, causing disasters even more severe than those of Chuang and Xian. Fortunately, Chairman Chiang supervised the army to suppress them severely, and they were gradually put down. The important plan for the future should be to learn from the past, eradicate corruption and local bullies, promote local autonomy, and implement economic construction, so as to eliminate the bandit scourge forever and revive the nation. Local autonomy is an important plan for political tutelage, economic construction is a source of benefit for nurturing the people, and corruption and local bullies are the cause of banditry in a negative aspect. If local autonomy can be completed, the people will have a correct understanding of politics and a deep belief in the Three Principles of the People, and the propaganda and agitation of the red bandits will have no means to achieve their goals. If economic construction can be promoted, the country and society will surely achieve prosperity, and the people will be able to eat their fill and keep warm. Who would be willing to take risks and seek good luck? As for corruption and local bullies, if they can be eradicated at the same time, China can never have the matter of officials forcing the people to rebel, and local autonomy and economic construction can also be accelerated and completed soon. Now, although the central government has set the above three points as national policies and gradually promoted them, the results are not obvious, and the day of success is far away. Wouldn't it be great?

Blocking and Suppressing the Remaining Bandits (4) Telegram to the generals of Guangdong, Guangxi, Hunan, Guizhou, and Sichuan to block and suppress the red bandits and not let them escape the net, said (Title omitted) The red bandits in Fujian and Jiangxi have been rampant for many years, causing great disasters unprecedented in history. The future of the nation depends on it.

In the future, we should make the greatest determination, do our utmost, unite with sincerity, and complete the work of settling domestic affairs and resisting foreign aggression.
