Hangzhou City Middle School Student Health Examination

Results Show a Large Number of Students with Intestinal Parasites

The Zhejiang Provincial Department of Education, in order to emphasize the physical health of middle school students, convened gatherings of principals and school doctors from middle schools in the provincial capital in October to discuss student health examinations. The Department of Education also issued guidelines for health examinations, instructing schools to comply. With the support of the Provincial Hospital, the Provincial Midwifery School and the Hygiene Laboratory served as institutions for stool examination. Results showed a surprisingly large number of middle school students in Hangzhou with intestinal parasites. The Department of Education has ordered the Provincial Medical School to provide effective treatment methods based on the type of parasite, for reference by school authorities, parents, and those in society concerned with the health education of youth, to encourage and supervise treatment.

Chiang and Liu, Representatives to the East Asia Higher Education Conference, to Depart for the Philippines Tomorrow

The conference aims to foster relations with the Chinese Communists.

Our country's proposals will be determined provisionally by the two representatives.

Chiang is scheduled to return to Shanghai on New Year's Day, while Liu will return later.

The East Asia Higher Education Conference is scheduled to be held in the Philippines on the 19th of this month. Our country's representatives, Chiang Menglin and Liu Zhanen, are scheduled to depart for the Philippines tomorrow. Details are as follows:

Departure for the Philippines Tomorrow: The Higher Education Conference is scheduled to be held from the 19th of this month, lasting for three days. Chiang and Liu are scheduled to depart for the Philippines tomorrow on the Dollar Steamship Company's President Jefferson. According to Chiang, the conference was initiated by the Philippines, and this is the first session. The purpose is to foster relations between China and the Philippines and to promote cultural exchange. The Ministry of Education has not yet formulated our country's proposals and will determine them provisionally during the conference. Chiang is scheduled to return to Shanghai on New Year's Day, while Liu will return later.

Chiang Menglin on Shanghai: A reporter from the Shanghai News Agency interviewed Chiang Menglin at the New Asia Hotel yesterday regarding the issues of banning dancing for university students and unemployment. (Reporter) "Currently, universities in Shanghai are strictly enforcing the ban on students dancing. What are Mr. Chiang's thoughts on this?" (Chiang) "Banning students from dancing in dance halls to avoid neglecting their studies is appropriate. However, there are currently no dance halls in Beiping, so there is no such movement." (Reporter) "What are your opinions on the issue of university student unemployment?" (Chiang) "To solve the problem of university student unemployment, we must consider all aspects. If politics are on track and various construction projects are initiated, there will be a large demand for talent, and the problem of university student unemployment can be easily resolved. If we only focus on the education aspect, there will be no solution, because there will still be no outlet for nurturing talent." (Reporter) "Mr. Chiang, you and Mr. Hu Shih once proposed to the Ministry of Education to reform Chinese education. Has the Ministry of Education accepted it?" (Chiang) "The previous proposal contained four points: (1) Ordinary middle schools and vocational schools should be run separately. (2) Middle schools preparing students for university should pay special attention to basic subjects such as English and mathematics. (3) Vocational education should not rely on schools; more factories and farms should be established. (4) The curriculum for primary and secondary schools should be reduced. These four points were discussed with Minister Wang in Beijing, and the Ministry of Education expressed agreement in principle and is currently implementing them separately."

Zhejiang Department of Education Stipulates Seniority-Based Salary Increases for Faculty and Staff of Provincial Elementary Schools

Since the elementary schools attached to provincial schools in Zhejiang Province were designated by the Department of Education to undertake guidance and experimental research work, the duties of the faculty and staff have been more complex and their responsibilities heavier. To encourage faculty and staff to work hard, the Department of Education has specially formulated Provisional Regulations for Seniority-Based Salary Increases for Faculty and Staff of Provincial Elementary Schools, which were ordered to be followed yesterday. The regulations are as follows: Article 1: These Provisional Regulations are specially formulated to encourage faculty and staff of elementary schools attached to provincial schools in this province to serve with peace of mind and work hard. Article 2: Faculty and staff of elementary schools attached to provincial schools who have continuously served at the school for three terms and continue to serve, and who meet two or more of the following conditions, are eligible for seniority-based salary increases: 1. Effective teaching methods; 2. Diligent school affairs; 3. Enthusiastic research; 4. Published works. Article 3: Teachers of elementary schools attached to provincial schools who meet the provisions of the preceding article shall receive a monthly salary increase of three yuan, which shall be paid from the provincial education funds. Article 4: Faculty and staff of elementary schools attached to provincial schools who are qualified for seniority-based salary increases shall have their qualifications filled out on the following form by the principal in conjunction with the director of the attached elementary school, with a written evaluation, and submitted to the Provincial Department of Education for approval two months before the end of each semester. Article 5: Seniority-based salary increases for faculty and staff of elementary schools attached to provincial schools shall be issued once at the end of each school year after approval by the Department of Education. Article 6: Seniority-based salary increases for faculty and staff of elementary schools attached to provincial schools shall be for a term of two years. After the term expires, they must be re-evaluated in accordance with the provisions of Article 4. Article 7: If faculty and staff of elementary schools attached to provincial schools commit any of the matters listed in Article 4 of the Regulations for the Appointment and Dismissal of Directors of Middle Schools Attached to Zhejiang Provincial Schools or Article 6 of the Regulations for the Appointment and Dismissal of Teachers of Middle Schools Attached to Zhejiang Provincial Schools while enjoying seniority-based salary increases, they shall be canceled. Article 8: The seniority-based salary increases for faculty and staff of elementary schools attached to provincial schools shall be limited to full-time faculty and staff of schools designated to undertake guidance or experimental work. Clerks and part-time clerks are not included for the time being. Article 9: The term of service for faculty and staff of elementary schools attached to provincial schools shall be calculated from the second semester of the 19th year of the Republic of China. Article 10: These regulations shall be promulgated and implemented by the Department of Education.

Huadong Girls' Middle School Holds Mandarin Speech Contest

Huadong Girls' Middle School on Beile Road in this city regularly holds various competitions to stimulate students' interest in learning. Competitions such as English recitation and essay contests have been held successively. Yesterday, a Mandarin speech contest was held. Each grade held a preliminary round to select outstanding students to participate in the finals. Each grade in junior high school had two representatives, and each department in senior high school (general, normal, commercial, and junior normal) had two representatives, totaling fourteen people. Sheng Youxuan, Guo Liangang, Shao Mingjiu, Lü Zhenkun, and Ren served as judges. The results were: first place, Qian Zangzhen, with the topic "The Current Crisis of the Chinese Nation"; second place, Hou Chenghua, with the topic "The Way Out for Youth During the National Crisis", and Wang Min, with the topic "Saving the Country Through Science"; third place, Chang Yurong, with the topic "How to Be a Middle School Girl Student of the New Era". The first place team was the third grade of junior high school.

Sports News

Changes to the 1934-1935 Women's Basketball Rules

Announced by the National Sports Association

Chapter 3: Changes in the Duties of Referees and Inspectors: (1) Acknowledging the qualifications of substitutes, and (2) Announcing time-outs when substituting players. The old rules assigned these duties to the referee, but they are now assigned to the inspector.

Chapter 4, Section C, Article 4: Add the following sentence:

When a player receives the ball while running, they may only use the rear foot as the pivot after taking two steps.

Chapter 4, Violations, Article 3, "Traveling": Add the sentence "Lifting the rear foot and jumping in place are included."

Chapter 4, Section E, Fouls, Article 1, (B): Add the third example and the full text of "Red" as follows:

Waving both hands in front of the opponent holding the ball, or intimidating them with both hands or other methods.

(Note) The above example may constitute a disqualifying foul.

Chapter 4, Section E, Fouls, Article 2 (B), "Charging": Add the following sentence:

Unintentional touching of the opponent's hand or arm is not considered charging.

Chapter 7: Add the following new Article 2:

If a "time-out" is called within the last minute of the first, second, or third quarter, the remaining time of one minute or less shall be added to the next quarter.

Chapter 10, Section A, Article 1: Add a new note after the first article:

The method of starting the game by throwing the ball should be agreed upon by both teams the day before the game.

Chapter 10, Section B, Article 3: The second paragraph has been revised, and the full text is as follows:

If both teams substitute players at the same time, the time spent by each team is limited to 30 seconds, and the combined time for both teams is one minute.

Chapter 10, Section C, Article 2 (A): During the center jump, the centers of both teams should stand with both feet firmly planted in their own half-circle in the center circle (the half-circle near the opponent's basket) (restoring the previous old rule).

Chapter 10, Section C, Article 2 (B): Add a note as follows: Except for resuming play after a time-out is called, no whistle is used for other center jumps or center throws.

Chapter 10, Section D, Article 1 (B) has been deleted, because the ball has already become a "jump ball". If a third party joins and physical contact occurs, it is an encroachment foul.

Last Night, Pirates Beat Qingguang 95-30

In tonight's two Western Youth basketball games, the competition between Jiangwan and Jinan in Group A is expected to be exciting. Yesterday's Seven Games of the Chinese Football Association: Results

Shanghai Middle School Athletic Association Disciplines Fuzhong

Resolution of Temporary Plenary Session

The Shanghai Middle School Athletic Association convened a temporary plenary session at 10:00 AM on the 9th at the National Sports Association office in Shenyuan. Attendees included Chen Rusong from Shanghai University, Sun Yiguang from Patriotic School, Yu Minzhi from Jinan University, Jiang Jingnan from Guanghua University, Chen Bingde from Fushi (also representing Minli and Chongde Girls' Schools), Xu Zheng from Pudong, Han Kuiyong from Fuzhong (also representing Minli), and Wu Lisheng from Shangzhong (representing Lu Xiangqian), totaling eleven schools and eight representatives. The meeting was chaired by President Lu Xiangqian and recorded by Jiang Jingnan. The discussion and resolutions are as follows: First, the incident that occurred on the 17th of last month during the football match between Pudong and Fudan Middle School at Fuzhong, involving insulting the referee, was discussed. After both parties, Xu Zheng from Pudong (also representing the Football Committee) and Han Kuiyong from Fuzhong, reported the actual situation, it was generally recognized that the person who insulted the referee was not a Fuzhong student, but an outside spectator who was unaware of the facts. Fuzhong teachers and students made every effort to stop the illegal act and protect Mr. Ni Xiaoben, who served as the referee. The circumstances were indeed excusable. However, since Fuzhong was in the position of host, this unfortunate event occurred, and according to the rules, it should also bear considerable responsibility. In order to prevent future occurrences, the following resolutions were made to punish Fuzhong for its negligence in prevention and as a warning to all schools:

(1) The Fuzhong school authorities shall issue a letter of apology to the Chinese Athletic Referees Association and Mr. Ni Xiaoben, who served as the referee (this Association will also issue a letter of apology to the Referees Association).

(2) Fuzhong's home field right is suspended for one year. All subsequent Middle School events scheduled to be held at Fuzhong will be moved to a neutral location, from December 9, 1934, to December 8, 1935.

(3) In the future, each school shall formally request the Referees Association or the referee by letter from the school authorities to show solemnity.

Furthermore, it was resolved that the regulations for this year's cross-country race should remain unchanged and should not be altered. The number of entries from each school shall be a maximum of ten and a minimum of six, as usual. The scores will be counted based on the first six finishers. At the same time, the Cross-Country Committee will be notified to implement this.

Free Talk

Works that Live Forever in People's Hearts

— Gu Xi

Reflections on "A Letter to Aspiring Writers"

It is works that should be written that have the capacity to have a lasting life among vast readers! That is, to write works that can live forever in people's hearts!

A writer must never write things that waste both their own time and others' time. Even more, they should not write things that are enough to harm themselves and their readers. The most important thing is that at the start of each writing endeavor, they should at least consider and understand whether what they are writing has strongly moved and profoundly enlightened them, and whether it possesses good and significant social meaning. Because literature, as Saneatsu Mushanokoji said, "is one of the movements that relies on expressing something from one's own spirit and finding one's confidant in the spirit of others." Therefore, it must be something that has burned one's own heart, shaken one's own soul, and moved oneself, and that one has integrated oneself with. Only then can it be generated from the depths of oneself and similarly burn the hearts of readers, shake their souls, and make them receive the same strong emotions. In this way, your work can find countless vast readers and live forever in their hearts!

To write a work that can gain a wide readership and live forever in their hearts is not an easy task. Unless it truly distills the author's full and substantial life, it is probably difficult to achieve this! Just saying that writing should "distill" something is already not easy. But the most important thing is to have something to supply for this "distillation." Thus, rich life experiences become most valuable to the author!

Every author should strive to become a person with profound cultivation, a broad perspective, and rich practical experience in life. Without this, it is as difficult to seek a great work from an author with a barren life experience as it is to seek sweet spring water in an arid desert!

In a letter to aspiring writers, the Soviet Literary Advisory Council tells us that Gorky's creations are unparalleled in popularity, influence, and social meaning "because he not only has the authoritative talent for description but also is extremely familiar with what he writes. In other words, it is because his authoritative talent for description is matched with the special knowledge of that description." This "knowledge of description," this "extreme familiarity with what he writes," is truly of utmost importance!

So, what can make us familiar with what we want to write, and give us broad "knowledge of description"?

To answer this question in a way that saves effort, I would like to borrow the words of A. Neverov in a novel. In "I Want to Live," when the protagonist ponders the question of "why we are unfortunate, while others are fortunate," he shouts out when he realizes the answer:

"Life itself gave me the answer and taught me. It opened me up with unbreakable truth!"

We can also say:

"Life itself makes us familiar with what we want to write. It opens us up with the most accurate and reliable truth, giving us the greatest amount of descriptive knowledge."

If Serafimovich had not personally participated in the revolutionary ranks, a great work like "The Iron Flood" would probably never have been "distilled"! If Gorky had not personally spent decades enduring a life of hardship and displacement, then "Mother," "My Universities," and many other of his immortal works might not have been discovered by us even now!

"The reason why Sholokhov's 'Virgin Soil Upturned' can portray the collective farm construction scene so realistically and skillfully is that Sholokhov studied the described environment very closely and carefully. The reason why Fadeyev's 'The Rout' can penetrate deeply into the masses of readers is that Fadeyev wrote the novel with materials that he had integrated, was moved by, and was extremely familiar with." It is said that Goncharov spent many years observing and working in real life to depict an Oblomov. From this, it can be seen that all great works cannot be obtained by chance. Writing a work that lives forever in people's hearts is not an easy task. The writer must concentrate their entire spirit on it, and the crystallization of the writer's true "whole self" must be revealed there. Only then can it become outstanding, profound, and appear great! This work is certainly not easy to come by, but we must strive toward the difficult and profound!

Laziness, timidity, and complacency will never succeed. Why do we, who aspire to write, not educate ourselves by delving into the vastness of life, making ourselves a person with correct education and broad experience?

"Seeking knowledge from the 'ceiling' and choosing materials from the 'fingers'" always leads to failure. Why do our authors create things that are alienated from themselves or even things that they know nothing about? (Why should those who only know West Lake write about Siberia? ...)

Every writer must write accurately and truthfully about what has moved them and is constantly active before them. Only by skillfully writing about something that seems to have the warmest feelings for oneself can it easily become a great work with solid content, strong power, and deep impressions, and thus penetrate into the hearts of people that cannot be easily reached, living forever!

The poet Balys Sruoga once sang such a song:

My song is made of pain and tears,

Forged by the sorrow of sleepless nights…

My song is full of cries, moans, and heartbreak,

Ringing out across the earth…

It burns the hearts of people with sorrow, making the happy feel sad;

That song itself is present above people's grief,

Ringing out and wailing endlessly!

Like that "song," which can "itself be present above people's grief, ringing out and wailing endlessly," let our writing also reach this state!

Literary Jottings

— Zaiqing

Gorky's memoir about the poet Alexander Blok tells of Blok encountering a street prostitute one bleak night. He held her on his lap with melancholy, spending the night in silence. The next day, without a word, he gave her all the money he had on him, and left with a heavy and gloomy heart.

Reading the diary of the French painter Van Gogh, I unexpectedly discovered a similar story. It said that when the painter Van Gogh was in dire straits, he went to a publisher to ask for a small loan to live on. The publisher was relatively enlightened, not utterly vulgar. After saying a few business-minded words, coupled with the conclusion, "Okay, people say you have talent. Here, here are a hundred coppers," he actually "bestowed" it.

From these two stories, we can very well see the greatness of artists, a kind of unattainable compassionate feeling. However, the problem also lies here. Blok gave away all he had, but could that prostitute save herself with his bit of money? Would that one night mean that, as our poet imagined, she would no longer sell smiles on the street? In fact, it is impossible. Van Gogh, when he saved a hungry old woman in the rain and snow, preferring to go hungry himself, that was his extraordinary quality. But, setting aside his own hunger, if he encountered a second, or even a third, such pitiful woman when he had no money left, what power would he have to help them? Those deserving of pity are definitely not limited to the one old woman he "bestowed" upon. "How could I obtain thousands of houses?", even if one had this thought, it would only be a "painted cake."

Poor artists, you should think on a grand scale!

Great Panic

— Ding Quan

The school inspectors are coming, the spot exams are coming, and the director of education is also coming. The students are panicking, the teachers are panicking, the business office is panicking, and the workers are also panicking. Students who usually don't burn incense are now forced to cling to Buddha's legs at the last minute. No one can be seen in the playground during the day. As soon as class is dismissed, everyone grabs a book and runs to a sunny place to sit down, eyes fixed on the book without turning. The few who remain in the classroom are also looking down, racking their brains. There's no need to call the roll at night; no one makes excuses to go to the toilet. Upon entering the door, they quickly pretend to pull up their pants when they see the teacher. Look, no one is whispering, no one is using yawns to express impatience with time. Everyone faces a book like a close friend. When the dismissal bell rings, everyone sighs that time is too fast. At this time, the students can truly be said to be cherishing every minute.

Wanting to look good is human nature. Who wouldn't want to have powder applied to their face? Therefore, various meetings to prepare for the spot exams and the school-leaving exams have been held, and naturally, some measures have been decided. Who doesn't hope that the class they teach will shine? Who isn't happy that the subject they teach excels? Thus, everyone puts in great effort, adding hours, adding handouts, warning students, and persuading students, and the students become vigilant (the students here are already very diligent), day and night. Originally, candles were not allowed to be lit after the lights were turned off, but this has been an exception for the past few nights. Originally, if there is something on one's mind, it is impossible to sleep peacefully, and the candlelight shines in the dormitory in the middle of the night. In the morning, before the sky is even bright, the sound of reading begins to rise on all sides. Even in the toilet, there are people muttering and spelling English.

Teachers are afraid that students will not be able to gain face, and what students fear is that there will be too many failing grades, demotions, and expulsions!

Students ask the teacher about the areas they should pay attention to, and the teacher gives a summary, at least this summary brings up everything that has been learned. The English teacher tells them to study English well, the math teacher tells them to work hard on calculations, and the Chinese teacher adds an extra Chinese essay outside of class for the students to practice (the topic is of course guessing what might come out).

Girls are even more timid, and their level of fear is even greater. They think in their hearts: if one person fails, one person is expelled, if one class fails, one class is expelled, if the whole school fails, even the principal and teachers are expelled! That would be terrible. Everyone would not be able to be together. We must work hard, strive for individual glory, strive for class glory, and strive for school glory.

The business office is also extraordinarily busy, planning this and planning that. They wore their legs thin with work, one thing after another. The glass on the doors and windows has been polished, new soil has been laid in the toilets, and not even a leaf can be found on the ground. Everything is fresh. Everyone is working hard, excited, serving the spot examiners, serving the school inspectors, and serving the Director of Education!

Until now, not one has been served, but many students are already sick in bed!

The Wheel of the Times

— Qian Zhe

In lectures on social sciences, it is easy to talk about the chain of relationships in natural phenomena. Some people say this is a "chain." However, as soon as the word "chain" is mentioned, some people think of "cycle." For example, "The way of the Three Kings is like a cycle," this is the "mantra" that a group of elder gentlemen are accustomed to saying.

To explain the "way of the Three Kings" is indeed not easy. Because the word "way" is so abstract, so mysterious; invisible to the eye, untouchable by hand, it is difficult to know where to start when talking about it. For the sake of "simplifying the complex," the elder gentlemen then give an analogy—"like a cycle."

Probably many people understand what a "cycle" is, so there's no need to waste ink explaining it. If you must explain it, then! Please look at the golden bangles that modern ladies wear on their jade arms, and you can understand what a "cycle" is like. To put it plainly, a "cycle" is a round circle that is connected to each other—it is impossible to tell which is the beginning and which is the end.

I also thought of a story—a teacher gave a question to students, saying that two rabbits, A and B, are chasing each other around a tree in circles. Is A chasing B, or is B chasing A? This really stumped the students; even the teacher who set the question might not have any "eight treasures" that could solve it.

The so-called "cycle" is probably like this, without beginning or end.

However, from the two words "cycle," we can easily think of wheels. Look at the vehicles on the road, the machine wheels in the factory, turning and turning, aren't they just like "cycles" without beginning or end? Some smart people, philosophers, opened their eyes wide and saw that the entire era was moving, like a wheel, never stopping. Thus, the slogan "The Wheel of the Times" easily spread and became a brand-new term.

The elder gentlemen who shouted the slogan "The way of the Three Kings is like a cycle" vowed not to bow their heads and also joined in the fun, shouting "The Wheel of the Times." So, these elder gentlemen can be considered "progressive," having already recognized that the times are changing day by day.

Wait a minute, the elder gentlemen are welcome to shout their modern slogans, but in fact, if we shine an X-ray on it, ha, this is just a trick of borrowing a corpse to return the soul. For example, they have been advocating some ancient prose all their lives, reprinting some editions of ancient books, and in their minds, it can be said to be a reflection of "The Wheel of the Times." In other words, they cite some brilliant classics as evidence, such as "Even after a hundred generations, it can be known." Why? This is all because "The way of the Three Kings is like a cycle" is at work.

The elder gentlemen think that the "cycle" is like a wheel; although the times are constantly turning, they are always moving back and forth in circles. In fact, although the wheel turns back and forth, the second time it turns is already different from the first time. (The first time it turns, it forces away the original air, and new air replenishes it). Moreover, "The Wheel of the Times" is not as fixed as a machine wheel in a factory; it is more like a wheel on the road. After making a circle, it has already moved to a new position.

It can be said that the Wheel of the Times is not as mechanical as the elder gentlemen's view of the times.

Tomorrow (13)

— (Joseph Conrad), translated by Wu Xiangyu

He took a breath, and he said very humorously, "Hey, lock the door. I don't mind if...you remember to come back and recognize me...um; what?...you can do it? In a week, you say? Humph, I dare say you can - but do you think I can stay in this dull, lifeless place for a week? Not me! I'll either go do hard labor, or join the fun, or have a place bigger than the whole of England for me to wander. Once before, I was in this place and stayed for more than a week. At that time, the old man advertised for me, and a partner who was with me suddenly thought of getting two pounds from him," he meant, he wrote some nonsense in a letter. But that trick didn't work out. We both had to leave - no one was in a hurry. But this time I have a partner waiting for me in London, and besides..."

Bethan Collier was breathing very rapidly again.

"How about I go knock on the door?" he suggested.

"Try it," he said.

Captain Hagberd's door creaked, his son's shadow moved forward, then he stopped, her ears sensitive to the sound in his throat.

"He's not very lively - is he? I hold him tight, I'm very worried. Many fellows often tell me that I don't know my own strength."

"He is one of the least harmful people alive," she interjected.

"If you had ever seen him chasing me upstairs with a hard leather belt, you wouldn't say that," he said, "I haven't forgotten it after sixteen years."

Another gentle, suppressed laugh made her whole body heat up. The knocker was making a rapid sound, he was even more nervous.

Since the short sellers did not cover their positions, and the retail investors' appetite was also satisfied, they had no choice but to gradually withdraw. Unless there is substantial progress in spring commerce, speculative stocks may still be unavoidable to lag behind. United Tanker is one such example and is worth purchasing. Oil Market: Jiaxing Has Poor Harvest, Hankou Has Shortage, and New Asphalt Sales Prices Soar

The new asphalt production is always the latest in western Hubei, Jingzhou, and Zhijiang. Therefore, the new oil arrives in Hankou after the winter solstice. However, Macheng oil is closer to Hankou, and it arrives in Hankou earlier. However, the body is softer and not suitable for candle making. Therefore, the candle making workshops in this city rely entirely on Zhejiang oil for supply, especially the Ben Che asphalt in Jiaxing area of western Zhejiang, which is the most suitable. The land is adjacent and can be transported by car. It arrives in the evening after early departure. Therefore, in previous years, there were thousands of pieces of Zhejiang Heben oil available after the light snow. With this huge supply, of course, no attention is paid to Han oil. However, this year's Jiaxing is a major disaster year, and statistics show that only 20% to 30% can be harvested. If it is calculated on the basis of last year, 30,000 pieces of Heben asphalt can be produced in winter, but this winter's budget is only 7,000 pieces, which is only a little more than 20% compared to last winter. I am only afraid that the local sales will not be enough, so I cannot transport it to Shanghai. It is also heard that Jing oil is being transported to Zhejiang for sale from Hankou and Shanghai to make up for the lack of Heben. And the Shanghai market has to purchase and apply from Han. In the era of alternating new and old oil, the new oil has not arrived, and the number of old oil stocks has been thin. Suddenly, it was snapped up by various gangs such as Shanghai, Suzhou, Hangzhou, and Jiaxing, which has a sudden upsurge. The demand exceeds the supply, and the market soars. Heavy Jing oil jumped from 9 liang and 8 qian to 11 liang and 45 qian, and Macheng oil increased from 9 liang and 6 qian to 10 liang and 8 qian. There is no spot goods available. All the transactions are on-road goods. After this action, the stocks were completely sold out, and the stocks held by the local merchants were also few. It is heard that there are no spot goods available in Hankou, and the sales prices have to be raised sharply. The current market price for heavy Jing oil is 19 yuan per shi, and the price for Ping Jing is 18.4 yuan. The oil market price in Macheng is 17 yuan. According to the calculation, the cost of Ben Che from Jiaxing to Shanghai is about 21 yuan, so it is far from suitable.

Hardware: The Factory Price of Round Nails is Slightly Loose

Recently, the factory sales of this factory's round nails have been very excited due to the interruption of the source of goods from the east and west, and the transactions have been unusually considerable. The sales in the Yangtze River area, the inland river gangs, and Fujian and Zhejiang are very good. The business in the north is weaker due to the collision of goods from the east. Other practical users all regard this as the only popular product. Therefore, the business of this factory's nails in this city is very good. However, the selling price is mutually lowered due to the establishment of too many nail factories (there are currently seven or eight companies starting production). Therefore, the standard price has been loosened repeatedly, and the recent secret market is even softer. It is heard that the market price is 5.75 yuan per barrel, while the secret market price is only 5.6 yuan (but it is limited to large transactions), a drop of 1.2 yuan compared to the opening price in the spring.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Idle Talk

On "Allusion" and "Plagiarism"

— Danran

The Chinese are the most adept at "allusion" of all peoples. Those who brew wine must find Marshal Du Kang, and carpenters must find the Immortal Master Lu Ban as their founders. It seems they cannot work in peace without something they can boast of as their "single line of succession." This is one example. Today, someone initiates an anti-superstition convention, and I can move a great many words to the podium. Tomorrow, someone holds a peace prayer meeting, and I can still give a "coherent" lecture. This is another example. However, these are still common social phenomena, and people generally are not surprised. If we pay a little attention, everything becomes laughable. I can point out another laughable phenomenon that is generally overlooked: the "allusion" of men of letters.

Men of letters cannot withstand the driving force of "fame," so they inevitably have to find ways to show off. However, our esteemed nation is a particularly antiquarian one. Those who love the ancient naturally despise the "now," and naturally want to "earnestly seek" from the "ancient." Thus, they must "allude" in every way possible, and find ways to find their "single line of succession." If you want specific examples, I can recommend that you go to a magazine company and browse for ten minutes. If you cannot find an example there, I can take responsibility for the deception.

"Plagiarism" and "allusion" are related. If you do not have goods, if you do not have ivory in your mouth, then presenting ancient and elegant scraps to readers who love the ancient is the supreme method. We have "heritage," and we can "search forward" with all our might. We do not worry about not having materials, and we do not worry about not gaining fame and fortune. If someone does not know what is good for them and wants to raise objections, then I can guarantee that you will encounter the number one ancient shield, and I guarantee that you will not be able to bear it.

If you love the ancient frankly, we will easily see it. If you are a young person, you will scold him as an "antique" and "stubborn." But if you encounter people who hold up the smokescreen of "organizing heritage," you will definitely say they "contribute to culture." So, everything requires methods. For example, some people's nude photography is vulgar, while other people's nude photography is art. If you understand this point, you will understand everything in this society.

Those who "allude" and "plagiarize" will "act as if something important is happening," release a smokescreen, and even "make rare things available," scaring young men. Although some people will find it "tasteless as chewing wax," they will feel goosebumps.

Group Wedding

— Youqi

Marriage is a troublesome matter. Not to mention the various problems after marriage that can exhaust you to death, even to the point of suicide. Even the preparations for the wedding and the holding of the ceremony can make you dizzy and spin around in circles.

But humans have this strange trait: whether before or after marriage, they know there will be all kinds of trouble, but when they reach a certain age, they still have to hold one, as if the trouble is fine, but the event still needs to be held. The reason is the establishment of a "family." In the eyes of modern people, if you do not hold one, it is secondary to yourself, but you cannot avoid being looked down upon, especially for poor people.

However, it is indeed too difficult to hold one. This era is shrouded in the poisonous atmosphere of capital. Marriages between the two sexes have also become somewhat commercialized.

In a capitalist society, money is the most important component. With this white and shiny weapon, it is easy to solve anything. However, these days are too depressed. How many people truly have the power?

Therefore, many people are shouting: "Advocate thrifty weddings!"

What is the response? We know that before this old latent power disappears, before the traditional concepts created by customs and habits are eradicated, the efficiency is very limited, extremely thin.

Page 18

If we pay attention to the advertisements in the newspaper, we can often see notices like this:

······We two have now progressed from friendship to lovers. We are scheduled to marry on a certain month and day. However, the national crisis is serious, and all cumbersome ceremonies will be simplified.······

Here, the so-called "national crisis" is, frankly speaking, "money crisis." Although this method has its own value, the grand occasion of a large banquet is inevitable, and who dares to say that the parties involved do not also want to have fun?

Now, the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau is initiating new life group weddings, gathering a number of couples who are preparing to marry and holding the ceremony together on a scheduled date, four times a year. Moreover, they are using the City Hall auditorium as the wedding hall, and the mayor and the director of the Social Affairs Bureau are acting as witnesses. This is enough of a grand occasion on the whole, and the fixed cost of the wedding is ten yuan per person, which is also sufficient to cope with economically.

We hope that this emerging method can be implemented as soon as possible, and can be gradually promoted to declare war on extravagant weddings!

The Sorrow of a Camel

— A Ping

There are no clouds in the sky, and the bright moon shines on the earth. It is quiet in the thatched house. Apart from the whistling of the night wind blowing through the reeds, the world seems to be dead. I am lonely, abandoned by this world; although my sympathetic owner, he occupied me because he wanted to profit from me. So every day he leads me to those roads that I am not used to walking on, to see those people I am not familiar with, making me a clown for people's amusement. Sometimes, for his business, I often suffer the blows of stones from naughty children. Naturally, generally speaking, there is also indirect benefit to me after the owner's pocket is warm and full, but I would rather do heavy work in my hometown, I cannot deceive myself as a puppet! It is said that there are many ways to tell fortunes, why did my owner think of calling on me alone? Or am I born too ugly, but humans love beauty, and the advertising of any industry must take beauty as a major premise. The little birds with red heads in the same line are for this reason, isn't that bird quite fun? I do not meet this condition, a furry long face, with a hunchback as annoying as an old man, and the way I walk is not beautiful, where do I start talking about this, but I bear the responsibility of advertising. However, it is a fact that many businesses are buying my furry face. Is there no fixed standard for human love of beauty? Thinking about it, there are special reasons, a tall person who exceeds the ordinary size is already worth admiring by his kind, let alone I am called a "beast"! Therefore, the owner's care for me is not as noble as his actions. Alas, I am lonely, I have left my hometown, left my companions, acting as the owner's puppet, acting as a plaything for the masses, I want to ask the owner to tell my fortune, can I be reborn in my next life? This is what I heard when doing business, people are asking what their next life will be like.

Today, I met old geese during the day. Since I came to this strange world, it was the first time I saw friends from my hometown. But the owner's business is important, and we had no room to say a word. We cannot enjoy the right to "meeting an old acquaintance in a foreign land"? I cannot help but hate my owner. If I were in my hometown, if I were insulted like this, I would definitely jump up bravely, pull open my legs, and duel with the enemy until he surrendered. My hometown is truly great, tens of millions of miles of boundless desert, where I charge into battle. Although our kind are also kept by the owners, we do not distinguish between "people" and "beasts," we help each other and live together, dealing with all environments. Sometimes we cannot find water and grass for days and nights, but we still try our best to move forward, and the wind in the northern border blows on us like arrows, we do not flinch, that kind of dauntless spirit is worth being proud of. But now I have been brought to Shanghai, which is known as the largest city in China. I am being played with, and because I am lying in this narrow surroundings, I have lost all freedom and become the owner's slave. I curse why humans cruelly abuse us like this, one day I will develop my authority and return to my hometown to live our own lives!

Now the fields are even more silent, the old geese should come to tell me some news from my hometown at this time, is the old owner well, are the companions well, is the hometown well? Looking up to the north, there is a glow of neon lights rushing into the sky, this metropolis is always surrounded by a colorful atmosphere, the old geese come here every time, I do not know for what, is it that the hometown cannot stand either? I am lonely, I have been abandoned by this world!

Child

— Julie

My wife has been in the examination room for a long time and has not come out yet. My heart feels like snakes are crawling on it. I am smoking and pacing in the waiting room. Our hope has been completely handed over to the doctor. As long as he diagnoses the result, we are like waiting for the judge's verdict.

There are more and more patients in the waiting room. My bored and impatient gaze swept across each of their faces, and I felt that illness was something that belonged to the poor; but the poor cannot afford to be sick! So I kept staring at the glass window of the examination room until my wife came out and the next number was called in.

There was a layer of fog-like sadness on my wife's face. I knew that the doctor had sentenced us to death. She slowly walked to me, without saying a word, and took my arm to walk out.

We left the hospital without exchanging a word, but everyone understood. What words to start with? This seemed to be an ironclad fact?

When we got home, the child jumped out of the servant's arms to hug my wife, and then I saw a trace of a smile on her face. This is a manifestation of instinct. Every parent loves their children like that. So why are they distressed about the arrival of a second child!

When my wife was first pregnant, it was already five years after we got married. She often missed it, saying that we should have a child. When she saw other people's children, she would snatch them to hug. Even the photos of baby competitions, she would cut out and hang in the mirror frame on the wall as treasures. So when the doctor diagnosed that she was indeed pregnant, she jumped up and down like a little sparrow, preparing everything after the child's birth. Like an elderly woman, she was so thoughtful, so cautious, and guessed that the future child would be like me, like her.

To be honest, this is what I expected too, but not as eagerly as she did. I felt that our small family was too lonely without a child, and after being married for five years, it seemed that there should be a child to decorate our lives. Sure enough, a child was born, and he was as lovely as we had imagined, with a round face and fat fists.

But following this joy, we were surrounded by a kind of oppression, which was the child's upbringing expenses. Our income, generally speaking, was still relatively generous, but since this child joined our small family, he has just turned three years old, and he has already occupied a considerable amount on our expense list. This is something we had never thought of before. Sometimes, we often quarreled over the child's expenses, and then came a feeling, how will we raise him when he grows up? This responsibility is on the shoulders of the parents. So although the child himself is lovely, many innocent children are sacrificed under these circumstances for this reason. Naturally, we are unwilling to do this, but the signs of the arrival of the second child do not allow you to bear his natural growth. At first, we hoped that this sign was just a sign, but time does not wait for people. Two months passed, and we were worried that this sign would be confirmed. But the heart that cherished the child was still consistent. From her usual tone, she hoped to have another daughter, but the economic chains were clearly that we could no longer have children. How did this sign scare us!

The result of the discussion, the doctor's diagnosis, this is just a one-in-a-million hope. Now this hope has been completely shattered, and a lovely enemy will join this harmonious little family. I looked at the child's joyful state in my mother's arms, and I could not help but worry about his future.

In Illness

— Li Ping

I received your third letter in illness! Ah Lin, the Ying you are concerned about is now seriously ill: ah! Although my body temperature is very high, I do not want to cruelly forget the love you gave me, and that you are waiting for my news in the distance. However, Ah Lin, you will know that the vicious doctor will not allow me to write letters no matter what! I am just struggling to get up in pain, suffering the nurses' prohibitions three or four times.

In fact, Ah Lin, I have simply lost the strength to write! My hands are terribly thin, Ah Lin, I can guess correctly, if you saw my thin hands, you would definitely cry non-stop. But you have to believe me, no, my spirit is very healthy. Ah Lin, since the second day of our little baby's birth, I have been ill for forty or fifty days, and I owe the hospital money. The accountant comes to urge me every day, but what can I give them?

You should know that a pregnant woman, as her body grows bigger every day: how can she continue to work more than ten hours a day as usual? I have stopped working, and it has been almost six weeks.

Whenever I am in great pain from the illness, I often silently mutter in grief.

- Come back - You, where are you! You are the one who can cure my illness! ...... Heaven! Where have you taken my beloved? Ah - I am shouting like this, of course you will not hear it; can

Page 19

But the patients in the same room sigh for my madness. Our sister Chun wipes away my tears non-stop.

- Do not be like this! Sister Ying, - Sister Chun always comforts me with a crying voice. - You should know that you have a husband who left you for the future of mankind, he cannot abandon his mission to take care of a sick wife, let alone he does not know that you are sick.

I stared blankly at his trembling lips. She continued:

- You should think like this: you should forgive your husband with pain! - I had to hide my head and cry to my heart's content. Ah! So I cannot be so childishly attached to you!

Today I reread your letter twice: every time I read it, a new kindness heavily presses on my heart. Only your every word can comfort my soul and make my faith in you stronger.

In your letter, I yearn for the scenery of a foreign land. You tell me that you are very healthy; however, I can imagine that your body is very tired, but your spirit is very happy. Because I believe that your career will give you unlimited comfort. However, our separation will make you feel very painful; but this personal trauma will never harm your great spirit. My Ah Lin! I know that we can fight for society and put love aside; we cannot wait for the imperialists to slaughter us under the flowers and the moon! What's more, your wife is sincerely waiting for your success. This love's encouragement can at least give you considerable excitement.

Furthermore: we are a young couple, and even more companions in distress; we should encourage our passion forward! How can I make you give up a greater cause for me?

Dear Ah Lin! We must always be firm in our faith and will.

But, Ah Lin! I still longed for you to return immediately when I was sick. Now, I have soberly overcome my emotions, and you should know that it is pathological and not worth your sadness. Do you know? A revolutionary fighter cannot be sad. So why do you tell you the truth? You know, this is my sincerity to you that cannot be hidden.

The doctor is advising me not to be too sentimental and to stop writing. I wish you success!

Storytelling with Stringed Instruments

Yao Xiao'an's Pearl Tower

Central and Western (1040) 10:00 AM to 11:00 AM

Opening "New Broken String"

Good things in the world don't last long. A wife's death leaving her husband is the most tragic. Few people invite him out. Sad, the door is locked with three yellows. Holding his son, he turns to his wife's family. Cold and desolate, he enters the inner hall. The wind blows the silk ribbon slightly. A portrait resembling his wife. A dim lamp burns before the spirit. A pair of flower shoes left beneath the table. He remembers his virtuous wife saying, "Wearing these shoes, I'll pass the Dragon Boat Festival." Now, she hurries along the road to the Yellow Springs. Thinking again, even more grief. He goes to the kitchen after a brief absence. Dust accumulates on the stove. The Kitchen God is enshrined in the hall. Half a tank of water remains beside it. With a thousand sorrows, he returns to the room. He sees the bronze mirror is also dim. Needlework and embroidery are piled on the table.玉偏方 is always kept in the drawer. Half the silk curtain hangs with silver hooks. 条条 brocade quilts are stacked on the empty bed. He wants to marry a second wife to raise his young son, but fears the stepmother's heart. Heartbroken tears on the mandarin duck pillow. In a dream at midnight, he meets his wife. He wants to talk about family matters. A black cat catches a rat, breaking the silver jar. Suddenly awakened from a fleeting dream. Midnight lamplight, a dream of wealth. The most bitter in the world is the widower.

"Falling Rosy Clouds and a Lone Duck"

Li Shao'an, seeing that Jiang Qiuwu has agreed, takes Jiang Qiuwu's photo to the women's orphanage to report to Dean Huang. Huang, hearing that Qiuwu is in the education field, naturally approves, and sends Jiang Qiuwu's photo to Feng Yuru. Yuru, upon seeing it, realizes this person is the one she's been longing for, but upon seeing his name, "Jiang Qiuwu," she becomes upset because of this.

Hua Mei (1060) 10:00 PM to 11:00 PM

"Man Jiang Hong"

Mo Xinye, to pay for Liang Qiushan's medical expenses, participates in Biao Jiang's "Mandolin" performance. Sure enough, after he finishes singing the lyrics of "Man Jiang Hong," the audience applauds enthusiastically. Mo Xinye then says sadly to the guests: "To save my friend's illness, I must now sell his beloved 'Mandolin'." The guests in the audience rush to buy it, and in the end, a young lady offers the highest price. Mo Xinye never imagined that this young lady would be Miss Li Taozhi.

National Studies

Ms. Wang Bingmei's Tang Poetry

Hua Xing (1260) 9:00 AM to 10:00 AM

Passing Jia Yi's Residence in Changsha by Liu Changqing

For three years, banished here, living a humble life,

For ten thousand ages, only the sorrow of the Chu traveler remains.

Autumn grass still seeks the one who has departed,

Cold forest only sees the setting sun.

Han Dynasty's culture was prosperous, yet favor was thin,

Xiang River, without emotion, how can it know condolences?

In the desolate landscape of declining trees,

I pity you; why did you arrive at the end of the earth?

From Xiakou to Parrot Isle, Viewing Yueyang, Sent to Vice Prefect Ruan by Liu Changqing

No waves on the sandbar, no smoke,

The Chu traveler's longing grows more distant.

Sunset at the Han Estuary, slanting over the birds,

Autumn waters of Dongting Lake, stretching far to the heavens.

Lonely city with its back to the mountain, cold blowing horns,

Solitary outpost facing the river, moored boats at night.

Jia Yi submitted a memorial, worrying about the Han Dynasty,

Banished to Changsha, pitied throughout the ages.

Presented to Chamberlain Fei in the Palace by Qian Qi

In the second month, the Yellow Crane flies to Shanglin,

Spring city, the forbidden palace, the morning shadows are removed.

The sounds of the Changle bell fade beyond the flowers,

The dragon chariot moves, the willows are deep green in the rain.

Sunshine does not dispel the hate of an unsuccessful career,

The Milky Way always holds a sincere white heart.

Offering poems for ten years, yet still not encountered,

Ashamed to face the temple leaf hairpin with white hair.

Shen Bao Architecture Weekly

The Prosperous Architecture of Soviet Russia

— Yan Ming

The importance of "architecture" in modern nations is clear to anyone with a basic understanding of modern knowledge. "Architecture" is not only a symbol of a nation's strength but also the "lifeline" of the entire nation's life. This publication has already provided numerous articles discussing the importance of architecture and raising public awareness of its significance. However, what we currently see is that the general urban populace, and even the entire nation, blindly praises urban prosperity. If asked why cities are prosperous and the close relationship between urban prosperity and architecture, they are simply ignorant and unaware. Therefore, it is still imperative to practically elucidate the relationship between architecture and urban prosperity to enhance the understanding of urban prosperity among urban residents and the entire nation.

For now, let's set aside political stances and purely from a technical perspective, discuss how Soviet Russia's prosperity and architecture are related. "Borrowing a stone from another mountain to correct one's own mistakes" might not be entirely useless for us.

It is undeniable that Soviet Russia has become increasingly stable since implementing its two Five-Year Plans. In Soviet Russia, both urban and rural areas are increasingly heading towards prosperity, contrasting sharply with the growing economic panic in European and American countries. We know that eighteen years ago, Moscow and Leningrad could barely be considered major world cities. However, they have now leapt to become some of the world's leading metropolises. Based on the current situation, they may even surpass London and New York in the near future. Why has Soviet Russia been able to progress so rapidly since the revolution? Why have Soviet Russian metropolises been able to independently move towards prosperity? The explanation for these questions lies entirely in "architecture." First, we must know that the late revolutionary leader of Soviet Russia, Lenin, once said: "Urban architecture plus electrification plus the Soviets equals socialism." The Soviet government accepted Lenin's statement, and during the First Five-Year Plan, the entire nation dedicated itself to construction. Needless to say, construction mainly includes architectural projects. Furthermore, it can be said that architecture and construction are one and the same. Now, let's look at the actual achievements of Soviet Russia's construction in terms of architecture. Since the implementation of the Second Five-Year Plan, the development of steel and heavy industry, the expansion of military industrial departments, and the rapid expansion of the gas and electricity industries have been achieved. With the concentrated efforts of domestic and foreign architects and engineering designers, over 900 factories for the aforementioned industries have been completed. The area around Lake Baikal in Siberia, formerly known as a wasteland, is now one of the centers of heavy industry, and the establishment of heavy industrial plants in the construction zone is countless. At the same time, Soviet Russia not only increased the number of factories in the industrial sector but also achieved the highest standards in factory construction technology. It has raised immature, small-scale technologies to new, advanced levels, preparing for further social construction. The achievements of Soviet Russia in industrial and architectural technology that most surprise European and American entrepreneurs are the great designs of the Dnieper Hydroelectric Station, the Stalin Gas Factory, and the Lenin Steel Factory. In terms of light industry, Soviet Russia's cotton textile factories, silk factories, textile factories, and all other light industrial sectors are also developing at the same speed, reaping tremendous benefits. All of this should first be attributed to architects, engineering designers, and countless construction workers. The vast achievements in factory construction have improved production capacity and ensured the stability of the lives of a large number of workers. In terms of agriculture, the First Five-Year Plan focused on concentrating scattered small-scale farming into vast collective farms and state-owned farms. Regarding the expansion of collective farms and state-owned farms, in just two years, 200,000 new collective farms and 5,000 new state-owned farms were newly built. These agricultural construction achievements have never been seen before in architectural history. Because these large-scale farms were built, productivity is stronger, and harvests are richer. The achievements in transportation infrastructure are no less than those in industry and agriculture. Since the beginning of the Second Five-Year Plan, the extension of railway construction in Soviet Russia has increased to more than one and a half times the original amount. At the same time, the construction of new roads and new heavy-tonnage bridges is also on par with the United States.

On the other hand, the cultural construction of Soviet Russia, reflecting economic development, is expressed in education. Every school, whether specialized or not, is established for the economic construction of Soviet Russia—the Second Five-Year Plan. Almost nine out of ten students graduating from schools each year are architects or engineering designers, responsible for guiding workers to build and consolidate Soviet Russia for the Second Five-Year Plan.

After seeing the actual construction achievements of Soviet Russia and their increasing prosperity, which are all created by Soviet architects and engineering designers leading workers, concentrating their efforts, and first focusing on "architecture," we should not only admire the success of Soviet Russia's construction or praise the greatness of Soviet Russia's construction. The main thing is that we should understand why they can achieve construction success? Why can they independently move towards the road of prosperity while other countries are going in the opposite direction? All of this is because their entire nation has modern architectural knowledge and can work practically to create today's achievements. Otherwise, instead of hearing news of rural bankruptcy, we see the deformed development of cities. Without actual construction, China's cities and rural areas will never prosper. At the very least, if the entire nation can understand the importance of architecture and its need in modern nations, then architecture may gradually become widespread in China as well.

Tomb of Unknown Heroes About to be Completed

— Ya Jie

On January 28, 1932, the Japanese Navy Land Forces provoked our defending forces on the pretext. Our side vowed not to yield and engaged them, leading to an unprecedented major war. Shanghai, a prosperous place and a commercial district, suddenly became a battlefield. The critical situation and fierce fighting were expected. Fortunately, our brave soldiers, such as the 19th Route Army and the 5th Route Army, fought valiantly, repelling the enemy and inflicting heavy blows. This excited and inspired the people of the country, changed international perceptions, and made the imperialist aggressors know that the Chinese nation indeed had good men. After the Japanese army suffered defeat, they repeatedly sent generals and mobilized troops, reversing their former belief that we were easy to deceive and striving to resist. Therefore, the fierceness of the fighting and the tragic circumstances were unprecedented. In particular, the battle of the 5th Route Army at Miaohangzhen, annihilating the enemy and killing the bandits, was the most intense and tragic. Both sides suffered countless sacrifices. As we approach the third anniversary of the January 28th Incident, should we not remember the sacrificing soldiers who fought for the nation's survival and the glory of the nation? Should we not shed a tear of sympathy to celebrate their undying spirit, and bury them to comfort the martyrs in the afterlife? Therefore, the preliminary idea of building a tomb for unknown heroes in Miaohangzhen, the battlefield, to show long-term remembrance and not to forget, arose.

Today, the cave that was destroyed by the war has been flattened. The trees that were ravaged by the war and aircraft have been replanted, and the atmosphere is new. The green grass, once trampled by countless soldiers and withered by the passage of tanks, has now regained its fresh green color, revealing its true face. Today, will anyone who visits the war zone and mourns the battlefield be able to see the desolate and ruined scenes after the war? The glory of the soldiers should be recorded in history, to be immortalized, to encourage the past, and to plan for the future. The relics of the soldiers should be deeply ingrained in people's hearts, the impression indelible, never to be forgotten. Those countless unknown heroes who shed blood and sweat on the grass will never be forgotten, representing the spirit of Chinese men. Understanding this, the construction of the hero's tomb by our national authorities is not without reason. The remnants of Miaohang have already been cleared, and the construction of the tomb of unknown heroes is currently underway. The completion and unveiling ceremony has been decided on the third anniversary of the January 28th Incident. The tomb's ground is shaped like a sword, and the memorial hall is built of pure granite. The hall is a rectangular solid, with a door opened in front, reached by climbing stone steps. Upon entering, one sees a spring in the center of the hall. In the spring, there is a stone coffin, indicating the resting place of the unknown heroes. The four walls of the hall are filled with commemorative charts, commemorating the detailed facts of the joint resistance against Japan by the 19th Route Army and the 5th Route Army, intending to inspire the masses, promote the spirit of heroes, swallow mountains and rivers, soar with ambition, and spread their names for thousands of years. At the lower end of the tomb site is a large gate, accompanied by a guard post and a garden.

If you follow the main road to visit this memorial building, you will see its elegance and tranquility from afar, with deeply shaded trees and a glimpse of the sword-shaped land and a magnificent building. The garden is filled with trees, flowers, and fruits. A visit along the path is particularly interesting. This memorial hall, with only building materials such as granite, green stone, steel bones, cement, steel, and iron, has already cost 100,000 yuan. Other expenses are not yet included. Fortunately, the amount of donations is considerable, which is suitable for strengthening the decoration and making it more spectacular. It is said that the designer is the engineer who planned the Greater Shanghai Plan.

Guangdong Bank's New Building Completed

— Yun

Construction cost: 200,000 yuan

Designed by architect Li Jinping

The area around Jiangxi Road in this city is lined with banks, known as New York's Wall Street. Pedestrians passing through this area are often unable to resist stopping to admire the magnificent and towering buildings, and they can't help but sigh with admiration. Now, the new building of the Shanghai branch of Guangdong Bank has also been completed, shining brilliantly and majestically, adding a lot of color to Jiangxi Road. From now on, pedestrians passing through it will be even more envious.

The new building began construction in February and has now been completely completed, which is one month earlier than the completion date stipulated in the contract. The efforts of the construction factory are evident here. Although the building has been completed, all the documents and books of the bank must be moved in at the end of this month. The total cost of the new building is more than 200,000 yuan, making it a fully artistic modern building. It occupies an area of about half a mu and is located at the northwest corner of Ningbo Road and Jiangxi Road. The main entrance and the high tower on the roof face southeast, towards Nanjing Road. The second and mezzanine floors of the new building are for the bank's own use, and the remaining six floors are planned to be rented to general businesses that want to set up offices in the central district. The interior floors of the bank are all paved with high-quality 12-inch square wood, with Belgian black marble edges. The walls are completely paneled with gray stone from the floor to six feet high, and from six feet to the ceiling, they are decorated with California paint, matching the paneling perfectly. The counters are also made of light red Carrara wood, with Belgian black marble countertops. The ceiling is decorated with gold paint, equipped with indirect lighting, which is elegant and magnificent. The new building was contracted by Jiang Yutai Construction Factory, and the installation of lead pipes and hot steam was contracted by Lengji Electric Refrigerator Company. Rosend Yangxing was responsible for the electrical installation, and Ge Liedao Steel Window Company installed the steel windows and doors. Other equipment, such as the elevator, was supplied by Wodes, the marble project was handled by Bierde Marble Factory, the imported hardware equipment was contracted by Shenchang Yangxing, and the domestic hardware equipment was contracted by Ruichang Hardware Factory on Sanma Road in this city. The Derbaude safe, which was installed, was contracted by Xintong Company. The exterior stonework of the new building was handled by China Stone Company, and the copper and iron projects were also contracted by famous factories. The new building was designed by architect Li Jinping, and Lennars of Shenchang Yangxing was the consulting engineer.
